A Dawnguard Scout

**Dawnguard Scouts** are [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") of any [race](/wiki/Skyrim:Races "Skyrim:Races") that sometimes appear at the fast travel arrival point just outside the [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") [keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"). They arrive in groups of three (one melee and two archers) and will attack immediately if you are allied to the [Volkihar vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan") and are a [vampire lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord"). However, they don't appear at all if you are a member of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").

Dawnguard scouts each carry a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe") and [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow"). They may also have a small amount of gold on them. They wear only [Dawnguard armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dawnguard_Armor "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"): light, heavy, or a mix of the two. Sometimes they do not have the helmet or the gauntlets.

## Notes

- If you attack them before they become hostile, you'll get a bounty in Whiterun, despite Castle Volkihar being in Haafingar. To avoid a bounty, wait until they become hostile, then attack.
- After completing quest [Destroying the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroying_the_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard") on Vampire side, they disappear permanently from game, after [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") lost the war against to [Volkihar Vampire Clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").

Dawnguard Vampire Hunter

The **Dawnguard Vampire Hunter** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") if you have accepted [Lord Harkon's](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") gift of [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"), for commited betryal to Dawnguard and completed [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice"). He carries [orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Writ_of_Dawn "Skyrim:Writ of Dawn") to "exact justice" on you for being a vampire. However, he don't appear at all if you are a member of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").

## Notes

- You can still encounter the Dawnguard Vampire Hunter even after finishing the Dawnguard questline for Volkihar Clan Vampires.

## Dialogue

When he attacks you, he'll use three unique lines of dialogue in addition to standard combat dialogue:

:   *"Halt, vampire!"*
:   *"Your end has come!"*
:   *"Light take you!"*

# Skyrim:Dawnstar Barracks

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Dawnstar Barracks ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar+Barracks)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Dawnstar Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Guard "Skyrim:Dawnstar Guard") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Wolf Queen, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v1 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v1")* | |

| [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | |

Dawnstar Barracks

**Dawnstar Barracks** is the living quarters for the [Dawnstar guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Guard "Skyrim:Dawnstar Guard"). It also houses Dawnstar's jail.

It is located between [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") and [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"). It is a two-story building with an upper balcony and direct access via a flight of stairs at the rear of the property. It consists of two areas: *[Dawnstar Barracks](#Dawnstar_Barracks)* and *[Dawnstar Jail](#Dawnstar_Jail)*.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Dawnstar Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Guard "Skyrim:Dawnstar Guard") |

## Dawnstar Barracks

Off-duty guards

The ground floor consists of an area for the guards to sit and relax, with access to the top floor via a flight of stairs against the east wall and to the jail via stairs down to the basement via a flight of stairs in the middle of the south wall. Under the stairs to the east are several barrels, including two containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). To the left of the stairs down to the jail is a set of shelves holding five bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and three common books, with a food barrel to the right and a rack hanging from the ceiling holding four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). To the right of the stairs down is a row of straw bales that continue around and along half of the west wall. There are two practice dummies set up in front of these. In the northwest corner are two food barrels with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") on top. Against the north wall is a dresser holding a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). In the middle of the room is a round wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of wine and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge").

The top floor is a sleeping area for the guards off duty. Above the stairs are two food barrels with two bottles of Nord mead on top. There are three single owned beds. The first is coming out from the middle of the south wall, the second is in the southwestern corner against the west wall, and both have [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") (both of which are non-respawning, unlocked, and contain leveled items) at the foot of them. On the floor, to the right of the first bed are two bottles of Nord mead and a common book. The third bed is in the northwestern corner against the west wall, with another non-respawning unlocked chest containing leveled items to the right of it. The door out onto the balcony is in the middle of the north wall, with a round table and two chairs to the right of it. On the table is a bottle of alto wine and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

## Dawnstar Jail

Dawnstar Jail

Entering the basement, the room is split lengthwise, with a single large cell behind an adept-locked jail door in the rear half of the room. There are barrels, crates, and sacks throughout the basement mostly containing foodstuffs. The east end of the room is partially screened behind wooden walls, beyond which are more barrels and a long wooden table holding two bottles of alto wine and one of wine, two loaves of bread, two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), several pieces of cheese, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), and several [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). To the right of the entrance is a large vat and a pile of firewood. The west wall has more bales of straw against it. To the right of the cell, against the south wall, are the evidence and personal belongings chests next to each other and in the middle of this part of the jail is a long wooden table holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a common book, and a copy of the [key to Dawnstar Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Dawnstar_Jail "Skyrim:Key to Dawnstar Jail"). The cell contains three bed rolls, as well as a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Wolf Queen, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v1 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v1")* partially hidden behind a pillar in the southwestern corner. This book is not classed as owned, so you are free to take it.

## Notes

- All cupboards, dressers, and end tables in the location are non-respawning and safe to store items in.
- The guard in the Dawnstar Jail area also has a copy of the key to Dawnstar Jail.
- If you pay a bounty in Winterhold in the [Skyrim Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"), stolen items will be confiscated and sent to the evidence chest here.

Dawnstar Guard

**Dawnstar Guards** are [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") who act as the military and police force of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). These guards serve under [Jarl Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"). Should the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") forces gain control of Dawnstar, they will be replaced by [Imperial guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Guard "Skyrim:Imperial Guard") under the service of [Jarl Brina](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis").

Dawnstar guards are clad in a set of Pale guard's equipment. This includes a [Pale guard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Guard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Pale Guard's Armor"), a [Pale guard's helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Guard%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Pale Guard's Helmet"), and a [Pale guard's shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Pale Guard's Shield"). They also wear a pair of [fur gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Fur Gauntlets") and a pair of [fur boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Boots "Skyrim:Fur Boots"). They are equipped with a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") supplemented with [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"). They also carry a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch").

## Dialogue

Below is a table of guard dialogue specific to Dawnstar Guards. All guard dialogue, including generic guard dialogue, can be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dialogue "Skyrim:Guard Dialogue").

**[Seren](/wiki/Skyrim:Seren "Skyrim:Seren")** [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") | | [Silus Vesuius's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius%27s_House "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius's House") | | **[Silus Vesuius](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius")** | | [The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall") | | **[Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder")**  **[Guthrum](/wiki/Skyrim:Guthrum "Skyrim:Guthrum")**  **[Ravam Verethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravam_Verethi "Skyrim:Ravam Verethi")** | | | [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall") | | --- | | **[Bulfrek](/wiki/Skyrim:Bulfrek "Skyrim:Bulfrek")**  **[Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn")**  **[Gregor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gregor "Skyrim:Gregor")** [HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") [[e]](#intnote_thane) **[Jarl Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Erandur")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") **[Gjuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjuk "Skyrim:Gjuk")** [[f]](#intnote_rise) **[Irlof](/wiki/Skyrim:Irlof "Skyrim:Irlof")** [[f]](#intnote_rise) **[Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(bard) "Skyrim:Karita (bard)")**  **[Stig Salt-Plank](/wiki/Skyrim:Stig_Salt-Plank "Skyrim:Stig Salt-Plank")** [[f]](#intnote_rise) **[Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring **[Borgny](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgny "Skyrim:Borgny")**  **[Edith](/wiki/Skyrim:Edith "Skyrim:Edith")**  **[Fenrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrik "Skyrim:Fenrik")** [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set") [[d]](#intnote_vigil) **[Harald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harald "Skyrim:Harald")** [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set") [^a](#note_sithis)This person only appears after the completion of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!").

[^b](#note_madness)This person only appears if he survives [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness").

[^c](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^d](#note_vigil)This person disappears after [Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil"). Harald only appears during the quest, other 3 people appear before the quest.

[^e](#note_thane)This person only appears after the completion of [Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale").

[^f](#note_rise)This person only appears during [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East").

# Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary

The entrance to Dawnstar Sanctuary

**Dawnstar Sanctuary** is a disused [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary on the shore of the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts") near [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). It contains only one zone, *[Dawnstar Sanctuary](#Dawnstar_Sanctuary)*.

The torture chamber

It was one of the first Dark Brotherhood sanctuaries in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), but has been abandoned for nearly 100 years.

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette")** [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Alchemy (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Alchemy (Master)") † **[Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") \* **[Dark Brotherhood Initiates](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Initiate "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Initiate")** [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") ‡ **[Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir")** [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Light Armor (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Light Armor (Master)") † **[Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")** † **[Torture Victim](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Victim "Skyrim:Torture Victim")** \*\* | |

† They move here at the end of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")
‡ They move here at the beginning of [Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head..."), once you have exited the sanctuary.
\*If he survived [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness").
\*\*After purchasing the torture chamber upgrade during Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head....

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness")**: Confront the traitor among the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.
- **[Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...")**: Restore the Dark Brotherhood's sanctuary.
- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Take the Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_the_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Take the Hidden Treasure")**: Torture the Brotherhood's prisoners for treasure.

## Walkthrough

|  |
| --- |
| During [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness")  It is built into the rock face on the northern coast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") with several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants growing around the entrance. The entrance is a black door similar to the door to the [sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It cannot be [picked](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") and has magical properties requiring the answering of a riddle in order to gain entrance. [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring"), the innkeeper at the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn"), when asked if he's heard any rumors will reply: "Everyone in town knows about the Black Door, and to never go near it", which adds the map marker to your map. You can discover the door and location at any point in the game, once discovered you are able to fast travel there, however prior to [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness") quest none of the three available options in response to the riddle will allow access. During the related quest the password is learnt by reading [Cicero's journals](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Cicero's Journal").  According to his journals when [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") first brought the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") from [Cheydinhal](/wiki/Lore:Cheydinhal "Lore:Cheydinhal") in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") he set up home in the Dawnstar sanctuary and stayed there for nearly a month before leaving to travel to the Falkreath sanctuary.  During the related quest when you arrive outside the black door you find [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn") sitting on the ground angry and bleeding. He's convinced he injured Cicero and possibly severed an artery, he thinks you should be able to just follow the blood in order to find him.  Activating the black door causes it to ask the riddle, upon correctly answering it will welcome you. You enter at the top of a flight of stairs, sure enough there is a trail of blood you can follow. At the bottom is a small brightly lit room with a small wooden table on the left with a complete unique [Jester's Outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Unique_Clothing#Cicero.27s_Boots "Skyrim:Unique Clothing") on top, including [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Jester%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Jester's Hat"), [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jester%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Jester's Clothes"), [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Jester%27s_Gloves "Skyrim:Jester's Gloves") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Jester%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Jester's Boots"). Behind the table, against the wall is a bookcase with five common books and several [ruined](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") ones on the shelves. To the right is an unlocked wooden door with a narrow table to the right with two more common books and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") on top. You can follow the blood trail, however it is fairly linear.  Through the door is a raised L-shaped section with a room below seen through metal bars. There is a round wooden table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top in front of you and a [sanctuary guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary_Guardian "Skyrim:Sanctuary Guardian") off to the left. In an alcove against the west wall, behind some wicker fencing is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush among other vegetation. To the right is a passage heading west and to the right of it is small set of shelves holding a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* and a [dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower. Beside this is a square wooden table with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an iron dagger and a single [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. A second set of shelves are to the right of the table with a bottle of each [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") on the shelves. Beside this is the top of a flight of stairs leading down into the room below, blocked by spears.  Heading west brings you to a wooden bridge spanning a circular room beneath. On the far side is another guardian. As you approach the bridge a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") will start poking several spears across the bridge from the sides, these can be avoided either with good timing or by jumping onto a ledge that circles the room. Once across, the spears stop. On the far side is a flight of wide spiraling stairs leading down. At the bottom there is a crate on the right with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top and in front is a table and cupboard. On the left is the room beneath the bridge with [oil slicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") on the floor and [oil lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging from the ceiling above. There are also two more guardians here. Take care however as there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") on the threshold to the room that will cause the lanterns to drop. You can use this to your advantage in dealing with the guardians. On the table is a map of Skyrim with a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")* and a copy of the [One-Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness")*. The cupboard holds a complete set of [worn shrouded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Worn_Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Worn Shrouded Armor"), only the [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Worn_Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Worn Shrouded Gloves") of which are enchanted doubling the backstab damage.  In the circular room there is a cupboard and three archery targets on your left, with a caved-in passage to the right of these. Among the rubble is a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungus. To the right are two practice dummies and to the north a wide passage. On the right of this passage are six weapon racks, another practice dummy and crate and table. On the crate is a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") with a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") on the floor beside it, while the weapon racks hold a selection of random [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") up to [Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Weapons "Skyrim:Elven Weapons") in quality. To the north is a set of shelves of the left-hand side holding a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") among items of clutter. Beside this is a crate with a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") on top. To the right another set of shelves hold only clutter. The passage at the rear leads up to the east and along into the room seen below previously.  As you enter the room two more guardians emerge and attack. On your left is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand and a crate beside it with iron dagger on top. There is a large broken circular stained-glass window in the northeast wall with an icy passage behind. On either side of this are picture frames with pictures of the black hand in red circles and the word "tenets" written beneath with numbering I—V, they are both very faded so the rest of the writing has been lost to the ages. The room has a raised section against the west wall with a large lit fireplace in the middle. To the left is an end table with a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") and salt pile on top, a food barrel behind with a loose piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on top. In the middle of the room is a long wooden table with two chairs, while against the east wall is a long end table with an iron dagger on top beside an ornamental vase. In the southeastern corner is a wooden door that is barred from the other side and on the floor to the left is an open crate containing a small coin purse under several items of clutter. Against the south wall is the stone stairs leading up to the raised section blocked be raised spears. There is a chain about half way up that operates these.  The blood trail enters the icy passage that heads to the southeast and then turns northeast, passing a small spur containing a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") and then turning northwest. There is a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") ahead with two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") nearby. Two passages run parallel to the northeast and both lead to the same cavern, but on different levels. The one on the right lead to a raised platform with a rock bridge linking it to a ledge along the east wall. On this ledge is [Udefrykte](/wiki/Skyrim:Udefrykte "Skyrim:Udefrykte") A large [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"). There is a dead goat on the far side of the bridge. Further to the right between a couple of stone pillars is an unlocked respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing gold with three [scrolls of Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fireball "Skyrim:Scroll of Fireball") beside it and beyond this is a dead deer and an earthen ramp leading down to the bottom level.  The one on the left leads to the bottom level and after passing under a rock bridge you can find the bodies of two [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") and a [horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"), as well as many other bones including mammoth bones. The ramp leading down from the ledge is ahead and in the western corner is a passage leading back into the sanctuary. As you re-enter, there is a passage with a caved-in section to the north and a pair of wooden door to the south. There is a blood splatter on the doors and through them there are spears blocking the top of a flight of stairs leading down with the chain on the right. At the bottom of the stairs two more guardians emerge and attack, while along the walls are wide shelves filled with coffins, these are mostly empty, although the odd one may be looted for a few septims. At the end the passage turns west and ahead three more guardians attack. Part way along there is a spur on the left with a master-locked respawning chest containing leveled items on the bottom shelf on the right. A short distance further along, the passage turns to the north and climbs a long flight of stairs. The passage at the top is blocked by more spears with another chain on the right. Beyond is a bear trap in front of an open door to a narrow passage, at the far end is a long end table with a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") on top and another black hand image with the tenets written below, this one is as faded as the two previous ones. On the left is the barred wooden door found previously and on the right is another wooden door. You will automatically sheath any [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and be unable to draw them at this time. Behind the door is a room with a fireplace at the rear and Cicero lying in front. Around the walls are several shackles and small units with sets of [torture tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Tools "Skyrim:Torture Tools") on top and holding the occasional leather strip. As you approach, Cicero will engage you in conversation. You must decide his fate. In the northeastern corner is another unlocked respawning chest containing leveled items, while on the right is an open crate containing two iron dagger and another leather strip. |
| At the end of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")  Upon the completion of [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"), you return here to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") who has relocated here with [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") and brought the Night Mother with them. Her stone coffin has been set up on a raised section, on the right by the bars overlooking the main room below. She is surrounded by lit candles on stands. The spear trap on the bridge, the oil lanterns and oil slicks, the bears traps and tripwire have all been removed or deactivated and the trail of blood cleaned up.  In the circular room beneath the bridge, where the caved-in passage was, has now been cleared and leads to some sleeping quarters. The patch of Namira's rot is still by the start of the passage, while half way along is a bedroom containing an unowned single stone bed on a raised section opposite the door. In the southeastern corner is a set of shelves holding a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a leather strip, a filled [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") in a stand and a sack of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). On the floor to the right is a basket containing a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), while to the left is an open crate containing two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and two pieces of [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"). Beside this in the northeast corner is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"). Opposite in the southwestern corner is a dresser containing random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with an iron dagger and three random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top, while in front, next to the raised section is another open crate containing a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"). Finally in the northwestern corner is a crate with a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") on top and basket containing three sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and a chair in front. [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") is often found sitting in this room.  The passage continues past this room and at the end is a dresser and another bedroom on the right. Along the east wall is a slightly raised section with two unowned single wooden beds, one in each corner. Between the beds is an unlocked respawning chest containing leveled items and an end table with an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") on top. Behind the bed against the south wall is a set of shelves holding a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), an iron dagger, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a leather strip and a sack of food, with two more leather strips in an open crate beside it. In the northwestern corner is a long wooden table covered in ruined books along with an empty leveled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a leather strip. Against the west wall is a dresser containing clothes with three iron dagger, a small coin purse and two loose septims on top, with a bucket to the left containing a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). In the southwestern corner is a round wooden table and two chairs with a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and a piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top.  In the main room the icy passage through the broken stained-glass circular window has been blocked up. The clutter and litter has been cleaned up. In the southeastern corner, where the previously barred wooden door was, is now an open passage leading to a T-junction with the torture chamber ahead. The passage to the south now ends at a dead end after only a few paces. The icy passage, cavern and coffin filled passages are no longer accessible.  Speaking to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") regarding the assassination of the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") will complete the quest, leads him to ask how much the contract was worth and to suggest visiting [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to purchase upgrades for this sanctuary. This initiates the next [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head..."). He will also state that while you are visiting Delvin he will see about recruiting some new [initiates](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Initiate "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Initiate") to the family. As you approach the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") on your way out, she will speak to you and [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") quest will initiate, this is an umbrella quest that stays active on the quests page for all future assassinations. Upon exiting, if you allowed Cicero to live he will surprise you and play a joke on you before entering the sanctuary to resume his duties as the [Keeper](/wiki/Lore:Keeper "Lore:Keeper") to the Night Mother |
| When Completing [Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...")  You can now purchase upgrades for this sanctuary from [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"), a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), just like any other player home.  Once you have visited Delvin and purchased at least one upgrade, when you return two initiates will already have arrived, they are [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and available whenever needed.  **New Banners:** Cost 1000 septims. Installs a total of twenty-two new banners throughout the sanctuary.  **Poisoner's Nook:** 5000 septims. Plants a small garden behind the wicker fencing on the raised area above the main room. It includes   - 2 [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") - 3 [canis roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") - 2 [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") - 2 [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") - 3 [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") - 2 [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") - 3 [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") - 2 [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot")   It installs an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") to the left of the entrance to the garden. On top of the lab are:   - 2 [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh") - 2 [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust") - 2 [Falmer ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear") - 3 [river betty](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty") - 2 Bottles of [Lotus extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Lotus_Extract "Skyrim:Lotus Extract").   **Torture Chamber:** 5000 septims. Refurbishes the shackles on the walls so that they work, in the room you originally faced [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") in. It comes complete with four [torture victim](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Victim "Skyrim:Torture Victim") shackled to the walls by their wrists, each of which, with a little [persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") reveals the location of some treasure. In addition two brand new racks are installed in the far corners of the chambers and a hot coal-filled cauldron with a heated iron bar resting in the coals on top.  **Secret Entrance/Exit:** 5000 septims. Replaces the circular stained-glass window in the main room behind which is a secret entrance/exit that comes out behind some rocks near the main road into [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") near the [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") and where the [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") camp. The window has the identical design as the one above the pool in the [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") [sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), behind which was where the [Night Mother's](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") coffin was stood. **Master Bedroom:** 3000 septims. Removes the dresser that was at the end of the passage with the two bedrooms off of it and adds a new bedroom, with the doorway being where the dresser stood. Opposite the door is a raised section for the bed, which is a double bed coming out from the west wall with a dresser to the left containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a medium and a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [scroll of fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fear "Skyrim:Scroll of Fear"), a [scroll of courage](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Courage "Skyrim:Scroll of Courage") and a [scroll of frenzy](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Frenzy "Skyrim:Scroll of Frenzy") on top. To the right of the bed is a set of shelves holding a leveled [potion of the berserker](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Berserker "Skyrim:Potion of the Berserker"), a leveled [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), a leveled [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a leveled [frenzy poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_Poison "Skyrim:Frenzy Poison"), a leveled [aversion to magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Aversion_to_Magic "Skyrim:Aversion to Magic"), a set of [shrouded robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Robes "Skyrim:Shrouded Robes"), a [worn shrouded cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Worn_Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Worn Shrouded Cowl"), [worn shrouded gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Worn_Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Worn Shrouded Gloves"), and [worn shrouded boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Worn_Shrouded_Boots "Skyrim:Worn Shrouded Boots") (see [bugs](#Bugs)). At the foot of the bed is an unlocked respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing gold and a pedestal with the unique [tumblerbane gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumblerbane_Gloves "Skyrim:Tumblerbane Gloves") atop. To the right of the steps leading up to the bed is a basket containing two samples of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") and a sprig of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). On the north wall is a row of six weapon racks, while to the south is a long wooden table and chair. In the southeast corner is a mannequin wearing a [shrouded cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl"), [shrouded gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Gloves "Skyrim:Shrouded Gloves"), and [shrouded boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") (see [notes](#Notes)) on a round table and in the southwest corner is an empty bookcase. Between these against the south wall are some crate with a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") on top one of them. All of the wall also have new banners on them. |

## Notes

- You are unable to enter the sanctuary without reading [Cicero's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Cicero's Journal") first. If you activate the black door, you will be given three dialogue options to try, but none of them are correct.
- Before you have completed [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"), speaking to [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring") at the [Windpeak inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") and asking about rumors will prompt him to comment: "Everyone in town knows about the Black Door, and to never go near it." Once you have completed Hail Sithis!, asking him for rumors will now prompt him to comment: "Did you hear? People have been seen coming in and out of the Black Door. Divines have mercy."
- Unlike the [Falkreath Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") can enter the Dawnstar Sanctuary. Also unlike the Falkreath Sanctuary, you can discover the map location for the Dawnstar Sanctuary before starting the Dark Brotherhood questline.
- When you first enter the sanctuary after speaking with the black door, the game will not autosave.
- It is possible for a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") to appear and deliver a letter immediately upon your exit from the sanctuary via the main door; after delivering your mail, the courier may turn and enter the sanctuary. However, the courier will not subsequently appear inside the sanctuary or back in Dawnstar.
- The shrouded robes on the shelf and the shrouded cowl, gloves, and boots are wearable, unlike the bugged worn shrouded items.
- All cupboards, end tables, and wardrobes in the location are non-respawning and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- The unequippable worn shrouded cowl, gloves, and boots that appear in the master bedroom will not appear in your inventory after you pick them up, resulting in the permanent occupation of 6 inventory carry units.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- If asked to wait somewhere, Dark Brotherhood followers never time out and return to the Dawnstar Sanctuary. This can be problematic because you'll be unable to pick up a new follower and may have forgotten where the Dark Brotherhood follower was left behind.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Dark Brotherhood members do not sleep in the Sanctuary due to not having proper sleep schedules. In addition, there aren't enough beds here and some are supposed to be reserved but lack their assigned ownership settings.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. Babette's bed and yours have been marked as owned to prevent NPCs who shouldn't use them from trying. One additional bed in the common room has been added to provide adequate space for sleeping.
- At the black door, the correct phrase sometimes will not appear in the options even after reading Cicero's journal. Loading a previous save should fix this.
- In the master bedroom area, jumping onto the corner between the platform and central stairs can cause you to fall through the floor and into the ice caves blocked off after the Sanctuary is reclaimed. You can escape this area by walking the way you need to go for [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness").
- The large weapons rack in the main hall below the bridge cannot be used to store player weapons.
- If the mannequin isn't on the pedestal, activating it can cause the game to crash. **?**
- The unequippable worn shrouded cowl may be missing from the master bedroom. **?**
- Plants in the garden may never regrow. **?**
- If you hit the torture victims with the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack"), the victim you selected may appear unshackled and immobile when the transformation effect wears off. Hitting them with the [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") shout can yield similar results. **?**
- Returning to the [Falkreath Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") after the Dark Brotherhood moves into this one will still cause the loading screen to say "The Sanctuary in Skyrim's Pine Forest is the Dark Brotherhood's last remaining refuge in all of Tamriel." **?**

Dawnstar

**Dawnstar** is a city on the northern coast of Skyrim, and the capital of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). It is initially aligned with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") under [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"). The city is a relatively small fishing and mining settlement with few services. The residents will report having [horrible nightmares](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare"), which some initially blame on a witch's curse.

For more information on Dawnstar, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Dawnstar "Lore:Dawnstar").

[^d](#note_vigil)This person disappears after [Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil"). Harald only appears during the quest, other 3 people appear before the quest.

[^e](#note_thane)This person only appears after the completion of [Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale").

[^f](#note_rise)This person only appears during [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East").

#### Daedric

- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.
- **[Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare")**: Relieve the people of Dawnstar from [Vaermina](/wiki/Lore:Vaermina "Lore:Vaermina")'s curse.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

| Giver Location | Quest Giver | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

## Notes

- With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, you can purchase [a plot of land](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall") in the Pale to build a house on. Also, two [stone quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") will be present.
- [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") granted upon completion of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")
- [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds a permanently disabled map marker for Dawnstar Docks.
- [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") is just south of Fruki's House, in the northwest corner of town.
- [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") is just east of [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"), at the east end of town.
- A blacksmith's forge and hide tanner are outside Rustleif's house, near the water.
- A tent is northeast of town, past the hill on which the lighthouse is situated. Inside, someone has set up a lovers' retreat, complete with two unowned bedrolls, a few articles of clothing, wine, [flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), and an [amulet of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Mara "Skyrim:Amulet of Mara").
- Dawnstar also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Dawnstar "Arena:Dawnstar")* and *[Dawnstar](/wiki/Dawnstar:Places "Dawnstar:Places")*.

## Bugs

- Ahkari's hidden [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest") in Dawnstar is accessible due to a bug. See [Ahkari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahkari#Bugs "Skyrim:Ahkari")'s page for details.

Daynas Valen

**Daynas Valen** was a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") who came to Skyrim in search of the [Gauldur Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gauldur_Amulet "Skyrim:The Gauldur Amulet"). He first heard of the Legend of Gauldur and the Gauldur Amulet 100 years ago, and since then he had felt its power calling to him. He became so obsessed that he dedicated his life into researching the life of [Gauldur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur "Skyrim:Gauldur") and his three sons [Jyrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Jyrik Gauldurson"), [Sigdis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigdis_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Sigdis Gauldurson"), and [Mikrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikrul_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Mikrul Gauldurson").

After learning of the final resting place of the sons and fragments of the Gauldur Amulet, he began his first expedition into [Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur"). However, he was unable to gain entrance without the [ivory dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivory_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Ivory Dragon Claw") and the expedition was put on hold. After ten years of searching, he traced the location of the ivory dragon claw to a collector in the city of [Bravil](/wiki/Lore:Bravil "Lore:Bravil") in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), who he then killed and stole the ivory dragon claw from. He then fled to [Anvil](/wiki/Lore:Anvil "Lore:Anvil") and boarded the [Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

On the Icerunner's three week voyage from Anvil to Solitude, he met an [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer") who was going to seek his fortune in the ruins of Skyrim with his companions, and invited them on his expedition intending to use them as fodder for the traps and [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") within the tombs. Unfortunately, things didn't go according to plan, and he died along with the adventurers in Folgunthur. In his possession you can find the ivory dragon claw and [his notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Daynas_Valen%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Daynas Valen's Notes").

## Related Quests

- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").

## Notes

- His [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Daynas_Valen%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Daynas Valen's Journal") can be found in the camp outside Folgunthur.

Dayspring Canyon

**Dayspring Canyon** is the wilderness area surrounding [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), accessed through a cave entrance southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

The canyon's narrow path

The entrance to the canyon is through a narrow fissure in the rock wall a short distance east of the path that leads up to [Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge"), along the road to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"). The fissure leads into a narrow crevice that eventually opens into the isolated canyon. It is the only available route to Fort Dawnguard the first time you go there.

## Dayspring Canyon People

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Dayspring Canyon | | --- | | **[Alvide](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvide "Skyrim:Alvide")**  **[Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)")**  **[Jayri](/wiki/Skyrim:Jayri "Skyrim:Jayri")**  **[Ollrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Ollrod "Skyrim:Ollrod")**  **[Sern](/wiki/Skyrim:Sern "Skyrim:Sern")**  **[Tilde](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilde "Skyrim:Tilde")**  **[Vori](/wiki/Skyrim:Vori "Skyrim:Vori")** | |

## Related Quests

- **[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)")**: Speak with the leader of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").

### Initial state

Waterfalls in the canyon

Once through the fissure, there is a snowy path heading east with a few [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes along it. As the path turns to the southeast, it widens to offer a view of a pool which is fed by melting ice falling as waterfalls from the surrounding peaks. The fertile canyon contains many fauna and flora, including [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") and [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), several types of fungi including [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") and [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), and many [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly "Skyrim:Butterfly") and [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") during the day, with [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") appearing in the evening and at night. The pool is full of [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)"), and there are [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") nearby. [Rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit"), [foxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox "Skyrim:Fox"), and [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") abound in the canyon.

The path leads down past the shore of the pool, where you'll find a rowboat and two racks, one holding seven whole salmon, and the other drying a net with two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels nearby. Next to the rowboat and the salmon rack is a wooden table with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") on your left. Past this point, the path turns to the north. Ahead, you get your first view of a fort to the northeast. Farther uphill to the north is a snowberry bush and an entrance to [Mossy Glen Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Mossy_Glen_Cave "Skyrim:Mossy Glen Cave"). As you near, the fort is identified as [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"). It appears to be a vast, sprawling structure. The path continues past the start of a wooden palisade wall, with some barrels of food behind. A [hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammer "Skyrim:Hammer") and a [saw](/wiki/Skyrim:Saw "Skyrim:Saw") are nearby, implying the palisade has been recently worked on. On your right is a wooden lookout platform. The path passes under an arch formed by a walkway far above. Beyond the arch is a campfire, with [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") standing nearby practicing with a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow"), and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") to the left. You can recover many [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt") from the tree stump Durak has been using for target practice. You can ask Durak what he's shooting with, and he'll give you a crossbow and 45 steel bolts. (See [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)") for a way to be given another crossbow and 45 more steel bolts).

Beyond this area is a fenced vegetable patch containing eight [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") plants, seven [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") plants, and five [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants. The path then turns to the south and approaches the entrance to the fort. On your left is another wooden palisade wall, with a gap in the middle. On the other side of the wall, most of the trees have been cut down for the construction. There are two snowberry bushes in this area, and in the northern corner, another entrance to Mossy Glen Cave. To the right of the gap in the wall is another wood chopping block and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). The first time you approach the fort, you will meet [Agmaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Agmaer "Skyrim:Agmaer"), who has also heard of the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") hunters and is looking to join. At the entrance, [Celann](/wiki/Skyrim:Celann "Skyrim:Celann") will instruct you to enter to meet [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"), their leader.

There are three balconies on the roof of Fort Dawnguard, accessible from the fort itself. One of them has two crossbows, 21 steel bolts, three [Dawnguard war axes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe"), a [Dawnguard warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Warhammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Warhammer"), three [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), two bed rolls, a small coin purse, a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), an [Amulet of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Talos "Skyrim:Amulet of Talos"), and copies of [The Talos Mistake](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Talos_Mistake "Skyrim:The Talos Mistake") and [2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1"). Another one has two more crossbows, 14 steel bolts, another Dawnguard war axe, a [Dawnguard helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Helmet "Skyrim:Dawnguard Helmet"), a pair of [Dawnguard gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dawnguard Gauntlets"), a [Scroll of Banish Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Banish_Daedra "Skyrim:Scroll of Banish Daedra"), two magicka potions, a bed roll, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"), and a copy of [The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v1 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1"). The third has three more crossbows, 16 steel bolts, three more Dawnguard war axes, another Dawnguard warhammer, a pair of [Dawnguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Boots "Skyrim:Dawnguard Boots"), a [Dawnguard shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Shield "Skyrim:Dawnguard Shield"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), three Dawnguard banners around the tower, 13 steel arrows, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a small coin purse, a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), a bed roll, a magicka potion, [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"), [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), a bowl of [beef stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Beef_Stew "Skyrim:Beef Stew"), and two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead").

### Later changes

At the end of the quest [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline"), a small group of vampires attack Fort Dawnguard. Their bodies remain on the ground until after the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet "Skyrim:Prophet"), when Dayspring Canyon undergoes a change.

The Dawnguard builds two palisade walls along the narrow path leading to the fort, complemented with *chevaux de frise*. The inner wall has a heavy wooden gate. [Tilde](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilde "Skyrim:Tilde") and [Vori](/wiki/Skyrim:Vori "Skyrim:Vori") stand sentry on elevated watch posts. [Ollrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Ollrod "Skyrim:Ollrod") patrols between the palisade walls. A safe distance from the palisades, two [Vampire Scouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Scout "Skyrim:Vampire Scout") scurry back and forth among the bushes near the road. During [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death"), four civilian refugees ([Alvide](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvide "Skyrim:Alvide"), [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)"), [Jayri](/wiki/Skyrim:Jayri "Skyrim:Jayri"), and [Sern](/wiki/Skyrim:Sern "Skyrim:Sern")) build a small makeshift camp behind the palisade walls. The camp has an Imperial tent, a wood chopping block, and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot").

## Notes

- If you use the snow on the east side of the mountain behind the highest balcony, you can potentially use it to walk along the ledge and drop down to the two lower balconies, and scale the mountain to get to the rest of Dayspring Canyon without backtracking through the fort. Don't drop down too far, though, or you'll instantly die once you land.
- The grindstone and tanning rack are on the roof of Fort Dawnguard, reachable by climbing the west stairway inside and exiting at the top. While these are technically in Dayspring Canyon, as opposed to part of Fort Dawnguard, they can only be accessed via the fort.
- Using the [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") here will clear away fog and rain, but not cloud cover.
- You can manage to escape the collision box placed around the map from the roof of Fort Dawnguard by hugging the mountain to the west. From there, if you explore the flat world around it, you can eventually find a strange map square, which is between [Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack") and the [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft") according to the map. It is modeled and will load its LOD and a rock tower; when approaching, it emits grotto sounds.
- Only two of the three Skyrim Atmospheres tracks that play in areas like [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") and [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") play in Dayspring Canyon; specifically, one of the two tracks that play during the day, and the one track that plays at night.

## Bugs

- If you go into the lake area, you may be able to go straight through the ice chunks. **?**
- Once the refugees arrive here and set up camp, they may simply idle where they originally were when you first meet them. **?**
- Barknar and Alvide don't have relationships set despite it being clear from dialogue that they are husband and wife.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Tower.png) | Nordic Tower: Dead Crone Rock ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Crone+Rock)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Dead_Crone_Rock "Lore:Dead Crone Rock")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 14 |
| Occupants | |
| [Drascua](/wiki/Skyrim:Drascua "Skyrim:Drascua"), [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")* [Pommel Stone of Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |

| South-southwest of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") | [Dismay](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismay "Skyrim:Dismay") |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |

Dead Crone Rock

**Dead Crone Rock** is a small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") inhabited by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), located south-southwest of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), just above [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt").

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Hagravens) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)")**: Do a favor for [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the Jarl of Markarth, by retrieving a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrolfdir%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Hrolfdir's Shield"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

## Dead Crone Rock

Upon entering, you will be facing a small stone table with a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), and a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") resting atop it, and a flight of stairs heading up to your right. At the top of the stairs, an unlocked chest, a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), and two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") on your right may distract you from the leveled [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") at the end of a dark corridor in a circular room to the left. Interestingly, two [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") can be found in this corridor, far from any water source. In the circular room are a table and chair holding a random potion of magicka and two bookcases containing a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), with a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") on top.

A spiral staircase in an alcove off the corridor on your right leads up to the second level, with a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus beneath it. There is a leveled Forsworn with their back to you sitting at a table in the first room. On the table are a [grilled chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Grilled Chicken Breast") in a wooden bowl, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a leveled potion of stamina. To the left of the table is a doorway to a second room where you can see another leveled Forsworn. To the right of the table, among some masonry rubble is another fly amanita fungus. There are also a large urn against the southern wall, an adept-locked wooden door on the eastern wall, and a gated doorway to the southwest. Through the adept-locked door is a dark corridor that leads to an outside balcony containing an unlocked chest, a large urn, and a bridge to a viewing platform which has a filled random soul gem and a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow").

Proceeding to the back room with the second leveled Forsworn, you will find a very long stone table with benches on either side with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") at the southwestern end. There are four bottles of alto wine, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") atop the table. There is a [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that spouts [flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") to your right as you enter; you can see this trap from the previous room through a window. There is an unlocked chest in the northern corner of the room with a corridor heading to the northeast; this corridor turns to the southeast and passes over a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") in the darkest part of the corridor. It then opens into a small room with a lever that operates the gate blocking the path in the first room; you can see this through another window. In front of the lever is a copy of the [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")*. There is also an unlit brazier containing a sprig of snowberries and two empty [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem").

Drascua

Backtrack to the first room and take the previously barred corridor. Follow the corridor up several flights of stairs as it turns until you reach an unlocked wooden door. Exiting through this door, you come to a broken exterior tower with wooden stairs rising in front of you. Halfway up the stairs is a second floor with an empty bookcase and two food barrels on your right, a table behind, and an unlocked chest behind to your right. At the top of the stairs you will see three spellcaster traps which all spout flames. Behind these is a stone altar; if you are here completing the [Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past") quest, you will find a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") named [Drascua](/wiki/Skyrim:Drascua "Skyrim:Drascua") behind the altar. There is an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") on the altar along with the [Dead Crone Rock key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock_Key "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock Key"), with a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for the [Dismay](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismay "Skyrim:Dismay") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") behind. A boss-level chest is on the north side. If you look back from the top of the stairs leading to Drascua's altar, to your left are some urns that might be easily missed in a small area at the top of the broken tower. Next to those urns lies a random soul gem. You can reach them by jumping up from the bookcase, jumping onto the wall that leads around the room, or using [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint").

## Bugs

- If you have already completed [Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past") and killed the Forsworn leader, [Drascua](/wiki/Skyrim:Drascua "Skyrim:Drascua"), she will not respawn and is not replaced by a generic NPC boss, which makes it impossible to complete [Trouble in Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Trouble_in_Skyrim "Skyrim:Trouble in Skyrim") if [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") asks you to kill the Forsworn leader at this location.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Dead Crone Rock
