# Skyrim:Dead Drop Falls

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Dead Drop Falls | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1HunterCave01, DLC1HunterCave02 | |
| Location | |
| [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 4 |

Dead Drop Falls

**Dead Drop Falls** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"). It contains two zones: *[Dead Drop Falls](#Dead_Drop_Falls)* and *[Dead Drop Mine](#Dead_Drop_Mine)*.

### Exterior

The cave entrance is in the northeastern section of the fort, between three practice dummies and the armored husky paddock. A few [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") grow on the wall to the right of the entrance.

### Dead Drop Falls

The chest

The waterfall hole

You enter into a natural cave system. Follow the passage, and you'll see a waterfall directly ahead. There are many types of fungi throughout the dungeon, including [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"). Above you on the left is a ledge with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). It can be reached with simple jumping; you can empty it when entering, or leave it until the end, as you will pass it on the way out. The only way to proceed is to drop into the hole formed by the water. You will land safely below in water; however, your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") won't join you (see [notes](#Notes)).

At the bottom, to the west is a section of dry land with a lit brazier and a narrow tunnel that leads up and around a circular, shallowly flooded shaft. At the top, the path joins a short passage and passes a metal gate, which can be lowered from the other side by exiting *Dead Drop Mine*. The passage continues past the gate to a concealed door with a lever on the left and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on a crate to the right. The door opens to the ledge with the unlocked chest in the first chamber.

Fishing supplies

Heading north from the bottom of the drop leads into a huge, shallowly flooded chamber, with many rock pillars sticking up out of the water linked by well-lit paths and earthen or rock bridges. Following the wall to the west will lead you to an unlocked chest. Returning to the path to the east, you will find a dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") caught in a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here; fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here. A search of the land beneath the pillars yields only a few fungi. At the top of the first ramp is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Across the following bridge, on your right is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from under the table behind. On the wooden table is an empty chest, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), with three [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and a sack beside it. The path continues to the north. At the bottom of the next ramp is another tripwire triggering a [crossbow mount](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow_Mount "Skyrim:Crossbow Mount") trap.

Continue up until you reach a raised wooden bridge in two halves, with a lever on the left. If you look to the south, you will see an archery target hanging from a stone pillar with a pressure plate in the middle of it, while next to the lever beside you is a quiver of [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt"). Pulling the lever will lower the second half of the bridge, but raise the first half; shooting the pressure plate with a bolt or [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") will lower the first half. Once both are lowered, you can cross. At the far end is another raised wooden bridge to the north, and a lever that lowers it in front of you. This forms a ramp to a ledge above. The ledge continues to the west and a tunnel blocked by a metal gate. Look to the south to see another archery target with a pressure plate in the middle. Hit it once to raise the first gate, but there is a second one behind. Move into the tunnel and hit the plate again to lower the first gate and raise the second.

You enter a cave with three pressure plates on the ground; on one of them is a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*. To the north is a tunnel blocked by another metal gate, above which is an archery target and pressure plate. On either side of the cave are ledges. If you climb to the right of the gate, you can easily reach this ledge, where you will find an unlocked chest. The other ledge is reachable using a single word of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"); however, there is nothing of interest on it. To raise the gate, you need to weigh down each of the pressure plates, then shoot the plate on the wall. This gate stays open permanently, so you can reclaim the items you dropped once it's up. Beyond the gate is a tunnel with another gate at the end, and above on a wooden platform is another archery target and pressure plate. Shooting the target will only raise the gate for a few seconds, so stand close and run or use Whirlwind Sprint to reach the tunnel in time.

Behind is a treasure trove containing an unlocked chest, with a straw bale to the right with two [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and two [ebony ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") on top. In the middle of the room is a long wooden table with quivers of [exploding steel bolts of fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Steel_Bolt_of_Fire "Skyrim:Exploding Steel Bolt of Fire"), [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Steel_Bolt_of_Ice "Skyrim:Exploding Steel Bolt of Ice"), and [shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Steel_Bolt_of_Shock "Skyrim:Exploding Steel Bolt of Shock"), and a copy of the rare *[Confessions Of A Khajiit Fur Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Confessions_Of_A_Khajiit_Fur_Trader "Skyrim:Confessions Of A Khajiit Fur Trader")*. Against the northwest wall is a set of shelves holding three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), one [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), a large coin purse, a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and four food sacks. There are two satchels containing minor loot attached to the left side of this set of shelves. To the east is a pile of sacks and three food barrels. To the right of these is a lever to raise the gate you entered through. A wooden door to the south leads to *Dead Drop Mine*.

### Dead Drop Mine

*Dead Drop Mine* is a small [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") mine containing four [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). You enter into a narrow tunnel heading south, and come to a room with several barrels and sacks scattered around. On your right, one of the barrels has a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top. Against the east wall is a long wooden table with three [corundum ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ingot "Skyrim:Corundum Ingot"), an iron dagger, and two pieces of [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") on top. To the left of the table is a small cage, and to the right is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a pickaxe on a crate. There is a corundum ore vein on the ground by the south wall and another by the west wall, with the final two corundum ore veins on a lit wall to the north. Between the second and third veins are a couple of straw bales, with another piece of corundum ore on top. To the south, past a couple of empty carts, is a narrow tunnel that leads to a wider tunnel heading west. On the left is a crate with three more iron ingots and an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") on top.

Ahead on the right are some wooden steps leading up and around to a couple of platforms, the second of which has an unowned bedroll, a copy of the unique book *[The Sultry Argonian Bard, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sultry_Argonian_Bard,_v1 "Skyrim:The Sultry Argonian Bard, v1")*, and a chair and a small square table holding a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a quiver of [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt"), an iron dagger, and two loose septims. Along the far edge of the platform is a pile of sacks, with two armed [crossbows](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") on top. Following the lower path, the passage turns south, passing on the right a set of shelves holding two [potions of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), copies of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")* and *[Troll Slaying](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Slaying "Skyrim:Troll Slaying")*, three pieces of [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin"), a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), and two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). To the right is a barrel with a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot") on top. The tunnel continues to a wooden door to the east that leads back into *Dead Drop Falls*. Returning to the first zone through this door, you will find yourself behind the lever-operated gate described near the start of the walkthrough, with a pickaxe on a crate just under the lever.

## Notes

- Followers will not drop down the falls with you; you'll be on your own after that point until you return to the start.
  - You can take them with you if you tell them "wait here" and then sprint into them to push them down into the falls.
  - [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") may follow you down, but may get stuck on the ledge just outside the concealed door.
- [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight") can also be used to trigger the pressure plates on the archery targets.

## Maps

- 

  Dead Drop Falls
- 

  Dead Drop Mine

## Overview

*Dead Man's Dread*

**Dead Man's Dread** is an ancient ship located within the [Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto") on [Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle"). It is initially filled with [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead"), but can be claimed as a player home after completing the related quest.

Once you have claimed the ship as your own, a map inside can be used for instant [transport](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#Dead_Man.27s_Dread "Skyrim:Transport") to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). You can also unlock the two other markers on the map to allow travel to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") (technically [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) and [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") by first discovering these locations. This mode of travel is one-way.

## Related Quests

- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

## Interior

The captain's quarters

What you'll see first after entering the cave is a path to get onboard the ship. After getting onto the deck, at your left will be the entrance. First sight you have's a steering wheel. Both sides will take you downstairs. There's a [Shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") and in front of it, to your left will be a room with 2 beds and to your right is the child's room, where you can find a [Scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"). The front door will take you to a hall with several rooms and some downstairs. If you go to the hall, first room will have 4 beds and several items and books. The room spotted at the left wall is a smithing room, and there'll be an [Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [Tanning Rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), a [Workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") and a [Grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), also there are 4 [Scimitars](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"). Across the hall entrance, you can find an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), an [Alchemy Lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and many soul gems and ingredients. Also there's another room inside this place with 2 more beds and another [Scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar").

Whether you go downstairs at the main hall or jump in the hole at the center of it, you'll see a tavern place, and deeper will be a storage for the tavern. Across the tavern is the captain's quarters with a single mannequin. There's a way left between the tavern and the captains' quarters, this path takes you to another room with 2 more beds. Finally, if you go right, you'll find the last room with 2 calabooses

## Notes

- The ship's cupboards contain unique clothing items added by this [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").
- Although Blackbone Isle has a map marker and can be fast traveled to from the mainland, you are required to take the boat back to [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear") to leave the island. This makes *Dead Man's Dread* particularly inconvenient as a player home, requiring three loading screens to reach via fast travel. The bandits at Orphan's Tear also respawn, meaning you will likely be attacked upon landing.
- Version 1.6 of the [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch") adds map markers to all 5 locations you can fast travel to from inside the ship. This mode of travel remains one-way.

## Bugs

- The Ghostly Remains of the [Ghost Sailors](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Sailor "Skyrim:Ghost Sailor") and [Ghost Captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_Captain "Skyrim:Ghost Captain") may not despawn and will instead remain on the deck. This happens when you read the [Pirate's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate%27s_Note "Skyrim:Pirate's Note") and return to Dead Man's Dread too soon to claim it as a home.
  - Wait for ten full days before reading the Pirate's Note and coming back to the island.
- The cooking pot in the kitchen by the bar on the bottom deck is set the wrong way round; activating it results in the player being positioned inside the wall, and leaving it results in the player being pushed inside the prison room. **?**
- The weapon stand in the blacksmith's room, aside from the three Scimitars already attached to it, may not be interactable. **?**

Dead Man's Drink Inn, Falkreath

**Dead Man's Drink** is an [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") in the town of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It is owned by [Valga Vinicia](/wiki/Skyrim:Valga_Vinicia "Skyrim:Valga Vinicia"). It is located near the center of town, opposite [Gray Pine Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Pine_Goods "Skyrim:Gray Pine Goods"), next door to [Corpselight Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpselight_Farm "Skyrim:Corpselight Farm"). [Narri](/wiki/Skyrim:Narri "Skyrim:Narri") waits tables, although she can regularly be found outside leaning against the porch fence, while [Delacourt](/wiki/Skyrim:Delacourt "Skyrim:Delacourt") is the inn's resident [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard"). It contains only one interior zone, *[Dead Man's Drink](#Dead_Man.27s_Drink)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Delacourt](/wiki/Skyrim:Delacourt "Skyrim:Delacourt") ([Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances"))  [Narri](/wiki/Skyrim:Narri "Skyrim:Narri")  [Valdr](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") \*  [Valga Vinicia](/wiki/Skyrim:Valga_Vinicia "Skyrim:Valga Vinicia") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") |

\* Appears here only after completing the [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)") quest.

## Related Quests

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.

### Exterior

It is a single story building with a raised porch at the front, wooden stairs lead up to the entrance and a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel is in the corner. By the southern corner of the building is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a couple of [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") that can be harvested nearby. Many of Falkreath's citizens congregate in the inn throughout the day and night.

### Dead Man's Drink

Inside Dead Man's Drink

It is a typical Nord inn, with a firepit down the middle of the common room. The counter is at the southwest end, with five long wooden tables along the southeast and northwest walls. There are three doorways leading to bedrooms, two on the southeast side and a larger one on the northwest side. There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") in the eastern corner and several barrels around the room. Behind the counter are two large vats with racks hanging from the ceiling in front of them. These hold nine [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), also hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). These are in front of a set of shelves holding bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). On the counter are several pieces of cheese, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. Under the counter is a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v6 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v6")*, five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") and several more bottles of wine and alto wine.

Either side of the doorway into the larger bedroom are a set of shelves holding several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), six bottles of wine, two bottles of alto wine, seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and three bunches of elves ear. The long wooden table against the walls typically hold bread and a selection of wine and alto wine. However the middle table against the northwest wall also holds two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and the table on your right as you enter, next to the alchemy lab, also holds a selection of cheeses and two salmon steaks. There is a basket containing three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") beside the firepit.

The larger bedroom is the room you will be shown to if renting a room for the night. It consists of a large double bed coming out from the northwest wall, with end tables holding a common book ([Mysterious Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Altar "Skyrim:Mysterious Altar") with the [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") Creation installed) and bottle of wine either side. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked non-respawning wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing gold, and against the northeast wall is a long unlocked non-respawning empty chest. There is also a small square wooden table and chair against the southeast wall holding a medium coin purse and four loose septims.

The two smaller bedrooms are opposite the larger bedroom. To the left of the left-hand doorway is a flower basket containing three [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). The left-hand bedroom contains a single owned bed in the eastern corner with an unlocked non-respawning chest and wardrobe at the foot of the bed and a small round wooden table and chair beside the bed. On the table is a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). The right-hand bedroom has a single owned bed in the southern corner, with an unlocked non-respawning chest and dresser at the foot of the bed and a small round wooden table and chair beside it. Both these chests contain only gold as well.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 6 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 8 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- All cupboards, wardrobes, and end tables in the location are non-respawning and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- Narri, as part of the [Server](/wiki/Skyrim:Server "Skyrim:Server") faction, is supposed to trigger the option to buy food from her menu when you take a seat inside the inn; however, due to her not being in the correct factions, no such option is available, so she'll keep asking you if you would like something to eat, with no possibility to reply.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  -  To fix this, add her to the Dead Man's Drink faction by targeting her and using the console command `addtofaction 000a6bfb 1`.
- Narri was meant to take over the inn in case something happened to Valga Vinicia, but she can't due to a backup alias not being defined properly.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- Valdr was supposed to be able to sleep here at night, but no bed is available for him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

Dead Men's Respite

**Dead Men's Respite** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").

The barrow is related to the first quest of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). The ghost of the bard [Svaknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Svaknir "Skyrim:Svaknir") is in the first room, and will lead you into the dungeon.

## Related Quests

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").

## Dead Men's Respite

Svaknir and the ruby claw

In the first room, you will encounter the eager ghost of [Svaknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Svaknir "Skyrim:Svaknir"). He is standing near the [Ruby Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Ruby Dragon Claw"). After he beckons to you, he will disappear, but will return to guide you through the tombs. Taking the claw will awaken four of the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") (which you can kill before you take the claw while they are still sleeping), as well as raise the gate directly across from the entrance. There are two small burial urns in the rubble in the southeast and northeast corners of the room, another in the northwest corner near an iron door, an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") to the left of the claw, and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") in an alcove in the southwest corner. There are numerous dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") throughout the ruin that can be looted.

To the northwest is an iron door. The door opens into a small, seemingly empty room, holding only a random sword and a random potion of healing. This room will eventually serve as the way out. Head back out to the main area and proceed through the now open gate. Follow the passage, watching out for a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") just before the intersection. From here, turn left, heading north. As the passage descends, look for two empty random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on a sideboard. Eventually, come to the end of the passage and a pull chain that activates several rotating doors in a row.

The next area is more of the catacombs. As you move through, you pass more rotating doors on either side and begin to notice a proliferation of spider webs. At the end, turn west and confront two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), then continue forward passing an alcove on the right containing a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"). At the end is an urn, and behind some webbing an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a shield, and two potions. Return to the previous room, where some thick webbing is to the south. Chop or burn your way through to enter a room ending in another pull chain. Again, this will activate several rotating doors in a row. As the doors open, two draugr will be waiting just ahead. Past the draugr is a [battering ram trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") triggered by a pressure plate. Bypass it to retrieve a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")*, a medium coin purse, a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a random empty soul gem.

Spiders nesting in the room with the trapdoors

Head through the passage to the north, encountering one more draugr slumbering in an alcove in front. At the top of the following stairs is an urn and a burial urn in the northeast corner. At the bottom of the first set of stairs is a pressure plate that triggers a [flamethrower trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues"). Bypass this and face a doorway covered with light webbing. Here, two frostbite spiders will drop from overhead. There are two bookcases with a random potion of magicka and a random empty soul gem on the shelves. To the right of the bookcases is a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"). At the rear of the room is a sideboard in the northwestern corner with a pair of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on top, and a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") and another pair of random boots to the right. Opposite in the northeastern corner is another sideboard with an urn and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top. There are also two lootable draugr cocooned in webbing on the north and east walls, and one lying on the floor by the sideboard in the northeastern corner. A further draugr corpse is lying beneath the first (shallow) floor grating, and can be looted with careful positioning.

To proceed, activate the pull chain on the wall to open the [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") in the floor to reveal a well. Drop into the well to continue. There is nothing of interest at the bottom of the well, and the way forward is to the east. Emerge from the water into a partially flooded passage and then into a larger cavern. A [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") is nosing about in the shallows, and a draugr is standing on a ledge, straight ahead overlooking the room, beside a soul gem. Another draugr will emerge from the sarcophagus below the ledge, and more will ambush you from the left. Collect a small coin purse and four loose gold coins from under the bottom of the wooden spiral ramp winding around the pillar to the right, then ascend the ramp. An adept-level [trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") iron gate bars the way across a stone bridge. Opening the gate without disarming the trigger in the bottom right-hand corner will set off four sets of [swinging blade traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") along the bridge. If you have to cross the bridge with the trap activated, a chain will turn it off on the far side, allowing any [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") you have to pass safely.

The magically sealed door to Olaf's crypt

Follow the next wooden ramp up and pass through a set of iron doors at the top. In an alcove to the right in the following corridor after passing an urn along the wall is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") built into a table, with a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") to the left. A random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") is on a sideboard to the left. Opposite the enchanter, to the west, along a short corridor is a magically sealed door and a sideboard with a stone bowl containing three [canis roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). A passage to the right heads down some steps. Here you will find more leveled draugr to deal with. At the intersection, first go to the left, passing a burial urn on a shelf to the left. A pressure plate that triggers a [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") which shoots Frostbite spells is in the doorway. It is easily avoided, but if you do activate the trap, remove the soul gem to the right to deactivate it. Another random empty soul gem is sitting in the same alcove, but may fall to the floor if you activate the trap. A dead draugr is on the floor, along with a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a random greatsword. A [scroll of Circle of Protection](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Circle_of_Protection "Skyrim:Scroll of Circle of Protection") is just inside the doorway on a plinth. Backtrack to the other side of the junction, heading north, to find an expert-locked door, behind which is a master-locked chest with [random loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

After picking up your goodies, proceed down the stairs on your left. As you enter the circular room, the iron portcullis closes behind you, and the other gates in the room will open, expelling up to five leveled draugr. If you are [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), and provided your Sneak skill is high enough, it is possible to avoid facing the draugr all at once. The first gate on the south wall, where two of the draugr came from, has an unlocked chest with an apprentice-locked trap that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). It is easy enough to avoid the spray of darts from the ceiling by opening the chest and then jumping backwards quickly. The other two gateways in the room hold nothing of interest, although an urn is found in the northeast corner of the room. Activate the chain to open the trap door in the center of the room, and follow the wooden spiral stairs down. At the bottom, the handle will open a section of the wall revealing Svaknir's body and the quest item *[King Olaf's Verse](/wiki/Skyrim:King_Olaf%27s_Verse "Skyrim:King Olaf's Verse")* in his hand. After you take the book, Svanknir's nearby ghost will disappear to go unseal the sealed doors. Make your way back up the spiral stairs to see Svaknir waiting for you. Follow, and he will now open the previously sealed doors which lead to a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps"). The puzzle requires the correct combination of symbols as well as the [Ruby Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Ruby Dragon Claw"), found in the first room, to operate. The claw reveals the correct order of the symbols: **Wolf—Hawk—Wolf**.

The crypt of King Olaf

King Olaf rising from the grave

The next room contains the tomb of [King Olaf](/wiki/Lore:Olaf_One-Eye "Lore:Olaf One-Eye"), and a whole host of draugr arranged in chairs on either side of the room. Most of the seated draugr are alive, and upon waking, will swarm you. Simply entering the room and strolling about is enough to rouse them. If your Sneak and Archery skills are high enough, you can pick some of them off before entering the room. After killing all of the draugr, Svaknir will bid King Olaf to rise, and upon doing so, King Olaf will attack. Svaknir will assist you in the fight, and as he is immortal, he can finish off King Olaf if the King proves too tough an adversary. After the battle, make sure to loot King Olaf's body for the key to the treasure room. There is a leveled potion of healing and a random filled soul gem on the center embalming table; however, as these will most likely get strewn about in the melee, they might be found on the floor nearby.

A [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for a part of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") is behind King Olaf's sarcophagus, in the back of the room. To the right of the wall is a medium coin purse in an alcove. King Olaf's key will open the master-locked door to the left, revealing an unlocked treasure chest, a random [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), and a random two-handed weapon. Opposite the chest, in an unlit brazier, is a large coin purse. To the right of the chest is a lever which opens the wall, providing a shortcut back to the small room by the entrance to the barrow.

## Notes

- This dungeon can be completed before activating the related quest. The ruby dragon claw and *King Olaf's Verse* will remain marked as quest items, and cannot be removed from your inventory until after [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo") receives *King Olaf's Verse*.
- It's possible to become trapped in Dead Men's Respite. After jumping down the trapdoor well in the frostbite spider room, the only exit is through the master-locked door near the word wall. On return visits to Dead Men's Respite, King Olaf is replaced with a leveled draugr that does not hold the key to this door. Thus, if you didn't keep this key from your initial visit and run out of lockpicks, there is no way out.
- This dungeon is often targeted for radiant quests; it is therefore worth noting the following regarding the boss/King Olaf's room for return visits. The grating at the entrance will not drop until you have advanced sufficiently far into the room. This usually happens if you advance much beyond the dragon statues on each side of the entrance. In total, there are fifteen live/sleeping draugr in the room, plus the boss draugr in the top sarcophagus (assuming Olaf was killed on your original visit). Four of these are immediately below the boss sarcophagus, five are to the left of the shallow pool, and six are to the right. Therefore, with a good bow or crossbow, suitable ammo, high sneak ability and archery skills, and good observation, it is possible to eliminate all the sleeping draugr before any wake up. You may then advance into the room (thus causing the grating to drop behind you) and the boss sarcophagus will open, making for an overall easier battle.

## Bugs

- If the dragon claw door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- Occasionally Svaknir will just sit by his corpse and not activate. Saving and reloading the game usually gets him moving.
- During the quest, King Olaf's verse may not be found next to Svaknir's body, with the indication arrow pointing to where it is supposed to be.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- The message shown when trying to open the sealed door here may appear regardless of which actor was actually trying to open it.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Dead Men's Respite

# Skyrim:Dead Scholar

## Overview

| Dead Scholar (RefID: 000B6424) | | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleElfHaughty](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty") | | |

The Dead Scholar

In life, the **Dead Scholar** was a member of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") who was exploring [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow"). He made it as far as a room with a locked gate, which he attempted to open with a lever. Unfortunately this triggered a hail of poisoned darts and resulted in his death. Before making his fatal mistake, the scholar had translated the runes that decorate the walls of the room and written them in his *[Notes on Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Notes on Yngol Barrow")*. The notes will prove essential in avoiding the scholar's fate. He wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots").

# Skyrim:Deadlands

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| ccBGSSSE067DeadlandsArena01, ccBGSSSE067DeadlandsArena02, ccBGSSSE067DeadlandsEntrance, ccBGSSSE067DeadlandsOrigin, ccBGSSSE067DeadlandsSigilAltar | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") | 4 |

The Deadlands

The **Deadlands** are a [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion") belonging to [Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Lore:Mehrunes_Dagon "Lore:Mehrunes Dagon"). This area of the Deadlands is visited during the quest [The Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Consequences "Skyrim:The Consequences") via the Oblivion Gate within [Red Scar Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Scar_Cavern "Skyrim:Red Scar Cavern").

The Dremora [Valkyn Gatanas](/wiki/Skyrim:Valkyn_Gatanas "Skyrim:Valkyn Gatanas") and [Valkyn Methats](/wiki/Skyrim:Valkyn_Methats "Skyrim:Valkyn Methats") must be defeated here. Additional leveled Dremora warriors and mages will also be present. Other than these enemies and a few flame atronachs, most of the danger comes from the environment itself: lava, aggressive [Harrada](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrada "Skyrim:Harrada") roots, and poisonous [Spiddal Sticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiddal_Stick "Skyrim:Spiddal Stick") are abundant. The more harmless [Bloodgrass](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodgrass "Skyrim:Bloodgrass") can also be found here.

Items can be found in two types of containers, Fleshy Pods and The Punished. The Punished are containers resembling a still-beating heart. Both types of containers yield enchanted weapons, gold, jewelry, enchanted clothing, rare ores, ingots, and sometimes spell tomes. There are 15 Fleshy Pods and 8 The Punished totalling for 23 loot containers in a relatively small area, making the Deadlands potentially quite profitable indeed.

## Gallery

- 

  Portal to the Deadlands

## Related Quests

- **[The Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Consequences "Skyrim:The Consequences")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"): Enter the Deadlands to face Dagon's champions.

## Notes

- The Oblivion Gate will remain open following the conclusion of the quest, allowing you to return to the Deadlands at any point. The generic enemies, loot, and ingredients all respawn.
- With [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") active, you will not suffer from the effects of [Hunger](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunger "Skyrim:Hunger") or [Fatigue](/wiki/Skyrim:Fatigue "Skyrim:Fatigue") while in the Deadlands. This is indicated in-game by the following message: *"You cannot feel hunger or fatigue in this cursed place."*[*verification needed — untested*]
- In total there seem to be 32 Harrada roots, 33 Spiddal Sticks and 40 Bloodgrass patches to be harvested upon each visit.
- The Deadlands make for a great source of [Daedra Hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") without using vendor exploits, upon the first visit there'll be 9 [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") enemies.
- One [Ebony Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") vein is far down the right-hand path where the road from the gate forks. From the pillars and throne, turn left and follow the path to its end; the vein is beneath some dead trees on the left. A leveled Dremora and two Flame Atronachs guard the location.
- Another ebony vein is near the cave entrance. Turn right immediately after exiting the cave and follow the cliff side, you will find 2 lootable Fleshy Pods (one standing and one hanging) right next to each other. A little past these pods are some dead shrubs and a dead tree, you'll find that there's somewhat of a jaggedy path there that leads up the hill. Follow the path up, you'll have to make a few small jumps over some of the rocks and shortly after you'll find another group of dead shrubs. Behind those shrubs is the vein.
- A third ebony vein can be found after crossing the second bridge and heading directly left. The vein is surrounded by shrubs.
- A fourth ebony vein can be found to the left of the cave entrance. Turn left immediately after exiting the cave and follow the narrow path uphill along the cliff. There will be a small alcove with the ore vein near the end of the path.

## Bugs

- Despite the Deadlands being an open world area, you cannot summon [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") here.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.
- The plants here are unaffected by the [Green Thumb](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Thumb "Skyrim:Green Thumb") perk.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.

The Dealer

The **Dealer** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") found behind a gated counter in [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den"), where she sells [Redwater Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Skooma "Skyrim:Redwater Skooma").

She wears a set of barkeep [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothing") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Clothing") and carries a small amount of gold, as well as a [Redwater Den Backrooms Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den_Backrooms_Key "Skyrim:Redwater Den Backrooms Key").

## Related Quests

- **[The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice")**: Fill the [Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice") from the Bloodspring at [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den").

## Dialogue

When you first arrive at Redwater Den and approach her, she can say:

:   *"Ah, welcome, welcome! I don't believe we've seen you here before, have we? You can buy from me, then join any booth you'd like."*
:   *"You seem tense. Join a booth and relax a bit. Or did you need another fix?"*

She can be asked questions when spoken to directly:

:   :   **What is this place?**
    :   *"Heh... wait, you're serious? This is the Redwater Den, purveyors of the best Skooma outside of [Balmora](/wiki/Lore:Balmora "Lore:Balmora")."*

:   :   **How about a sample? (Persuade)**
    :   *"Since it's your first time... sure. Find a booth and enjoy."*

:   :   **What is so special about your skooma?**
    :   *"The secret is our mystic Redwater Spring. The magic in the waters opens the mind to experience Skooma in a way like never before."*

If asked again:

:   **How about a sample? (Persuade)**
:   *"Well... so long as you don't tell anyone. Here take it and slip into a booth before someone notices."* (Success)

:   *"How about you pay for your habit like everybody else. We're not running a charity here."* (Failure)

When you leave Redwater Den, she'll call out to you as you go:

:   *"Be sure to enjoy some of our Redwater Skooma before you leave."*
:   *"Don't leave, you'd have better dreams here..."*
:   *"Fine, suit yourself."*

## Conversations

She can be overheard speaking to a vampire:

:   **Dealer**: *"That's the last of them. Poor sods can't resist after they get a taste of your dosed Skooma."*
:   **Vampire**: *"The water from the spring makes the skooma so much more potent, we'll have all the thralls we'll ever need. Good thing the boss heard that old farmer running his mouth off in the tavern about finding this place."*

## Notes

- According to the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Kit "Skyrim:Creation Kit"), her face data is copied from the [Voice of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_of_Namira "Skyrim:Voice of Namira") NPC `DA11VoiceofNamira`.

## Overview

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire") | | → Next | [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") | | |

Astrid performing the Black Sacrament using her own body in the ritual

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter the [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary").
2. Assist the survivors.
3. Hide in the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother")'s coffin.
4. Kill the [traitor](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid").
5. Return to the Night Mother.

### Welcome Home

The Sanctuary is under attack!

There should be several guards outside the sanctuary when you approach it, along with the horses and carriages that they arrived in. Deal with them and head inside the sanctuary. [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex") can be found dead outside, pinned against a tree by arrows. There are also several stacks of barrels holding oil, hinting at the way the Penitus Oculatus plans on destroying the sanctuary.

When you enter the Sanctuary, you will notice the entire place is on fire and structurally unsound. Close to the entrance, you will overhear two members of Penitus Oculatus discussing who among the Dark Brotherhood turned traitor. Next to them you will find the body of [Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara"). After their conversation, they will head towards you. Deal with them as you see fit. Astrid's and Arnbjorn's rooms are empty, so head down the stairs into the central room of the sanctuary. You will find [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn") in his werewolf form fighting Penitus Oculatus agents. You can try to help him, but his death is scripted and he will die even if you kill the agents around him. There is no way for you to save him. The corpse of [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella") lies in the next room, as does [Lis](/wiki/Skyrim:Lis "Skyrim:Lis").

### The Burning Brotherhood

Arnbjorn goes wild as a werewolf

Continue through the sanctuary, avoiding the flames until you find [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"). When you find him, he is locked in a duel with one of the agents, [Arcturus](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcturus "Skyrim:Arcturus"). Assist him by killing his attacker and talk to him. His concerns that you might be the traitor are erased when you save him. Follow him in his search for an escape. As you follow him while he searches for a way out, you should run past the room with the Night Mother. She will call out to you, telling you the only safe place is in her coffin. Make sure Nazir is out of combat, then run and open the Night Mother's coffin. Walk into it, and it will close around you.

In the darkness of the coffin you will hear explosions and sounds of the sanctuary coming down around you. After they end, you will hear the voices of [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") and [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") talking as Nazir tries to unearth you. When Nazir opens the coffin, you find yourself in the main room of the sanctuary. Apparently, in the explosions, the coffin was thrown through the stained glass window. After you step out of the coffin and talk to the two survivors, the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") will talk to you once again and inform you that [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") is still alive. She will ask you to find her. Nazir and Babette will follow you after you inform them of what you've just heard.

### Burned Beyond Recognition

The Night Mother tells you to go find Astrid

Take the stairs up to Astrid's old chambers and you will see a horrifically burned Astrid stretched out on the floor in her hidden chamber with candles surrounding her. She has performed the Black Sacrament, prayed to the Night Mother and placed herself in the center of the ritual with the [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe") (her symbol of status) beside her. Astrid reveals that she is the traitor. She betrayed you because she wanted things to go back to normal with the Dark Brotherhood. She was skeptical of Cicero and the Night Mother and envious of you for being named the Listener. With her last moments, burned and dying, she performed the Black Sacrament on herself and asked for a contract. When you arrived, her skepticism of the Night Mother disappeared, since she knows that her prayers were heard.

She reveals that what she prayed for was a mercy killing. She wants to be put out of her misery. You can retrieve the Blade of Woe found next to the dying Astrid, as an optional step. Once you kill Astrid, she will thank you with her dying breath and the quest will update and direct you to return to the Night Mother (in her coffin). Nazir and Babette will comment on her death with anger and pity for their former leader. Once you return, the Night Mother will talk to you, instructing you to fulfill the Brotherhood's contract to kill the Emperor. She suggests talking to [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") in Whiterun, but to let Nazir know of your plans first. Hence begins the next quest, [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!").

## Notes

- Even a non-offensive spell, such as Healing Hands, will kill Astrid after she performs the Black Sacrament. Non-offensive powers, such as Voice of the Emperor, will also work for this purpose.
- If you pickpocket Astrid before joining the Brotherhood and steal the Blade of Woe and then do this quest you can have two Blades of Woe.
- If you attempt to pickpocket Astrid and fail, she will stand up and attack, though she will remain in her burned down state and can still be eliminated.
- After killing Astrid, her body can be resurrected with spells or powers like any other body. She will not have any dialogue in this state.
- If you have any valuables stored in the sleeping area of the sanctuary, be sure to retrieve them after you save Nazir. Once you emerge from the Night Mother's coffin you will not be able to access that area again.

## Bugs

- You may become stuck in the Night Mother's coffin.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- After getting out of the Night Mother's coffin and speaking to Astrid, you may be frozen and unable to do anything, and you will be unable to receive the Blade of Woe and kill Astrid. If this happens, reload a previous save.
- There is a glitch in which you hear everything twice after entering the Night Mother's Coffin. It resets after Nazir releases you. **?**
- The dead Veezara might spawn unclothed.
- If you try to access the Night Mother's coffin as a werewolf, the coffin will never close, even after you have reverted back to your normal self. **?**
- When you must kill Astrid, if you fail a reverse-pickpocket attempt on her, she will jump up and start to attack you.
- When you have to assist Nazir, sometimes the agent he is supposed to be fighting doesn't spawn, despite the arrow pointing to where he should be. **?**
  - Reloading a previous save should fix this.
- Nazir may become invisible after this quest ends and the next one starts. **?**
  - Exiting and entering the Sanctuary will fix this.
- In some instances, if using a spell that is not intended to damage your opponent on Astrid, such as soul trap, she will stand up from her position and will attempt to attack, only to die immediately.
- A copy of the book *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")* was also intended to be there with the [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") sample when Astrid performs the Black Sacrament on herself. Unfortunately, the book disappears once the Sacrament scene is finished due to an improper enable parent setup.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you picked up the Unusual Gem from the sanctuary earlier in the quest line, it may respawn during this quest and can be picked up again. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Death Incarnate (DB10) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I have returned to the Sanctuary in the midst of the Penitus Oculatus' assault. I must assist my fellow Family members any way I can. *Objective 10:* Enter the Sanctuary |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Search for survivors |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Kill the Legion soldiers inside the Sanctuary (<Global=DB10LegionAttackerDeadCount>/5) |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Kill Nazir's attacker! |
| 35 |  | *Objective 35:* Speak with Nazir |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Escape the Sanctuary |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Embrace the Night Mother |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Talk to Astrid |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Kill Astrid  *Objective 81:* (Optional) Retrieve the Blade of Woe |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Return to the Night Mother |
| 200 | ☑ | Not only have the Penitus Oculatus killed most of the Family members and burned the Sanctuary, Astrid also revealed herself to be the one who betrayed me. But there is still hope - the Emperor is still in Skyrim, and I have a chance to fulfill my contract with Amaund Motierre. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 7, 55, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB10 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB10`.

The resting place of the King of Ghosts

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note:** You must be level 36 before you can start this quest.

1. (*Optional*) Read *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*.
2. Find the [treasure map](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Treasure_Map "Skyrim:Deathbrand Treasure Map").
3. Locate the four ancient chests containing the pieces of [Deathbrand armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Armor "Skyrim:Deathbrand Armor").
4. Explore [Gyldenhul Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow").
5. Defeat [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand") and his crew.

### Tale of Treasure

[Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Lore:Haknir_Death-Brand "Lore:Haknir Death-Brand") was known for rages and fits of madness, and he delighted in torture and murder for its own sake. He was said to have lived an unnaturally long life, and displayed a terrible scar on his face known as "the Deathbrand", which no man could look upon without flinching. Due to the terrible scar, some thought of him as a Daedra while others spoke of a pact he made with [Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Mehrunes Dagon"), calling the scar a seal between him and the Prince of Destruction. Before his death, he told his crew that none were worthy to be his successor or have his treasure. He placed a curse on his [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Armor "Skyrim:Deathbrand Armor") and his scimitars, [Bloodscythe](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodscythe "Skyrim:Bloodscythe") and [Soulrender](/wiki/Skyrim:Soulrender "Skyrim:Soulrender"). He commanded a crewman to bury his armor in four separate locations on Solstheim, each marked by a [map](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Treasure_Map "Skyrim:Deathbrand Treasure Map"), before sealing him in his tomb at Gyldenhul Barrow along with all his treasure.

This story was written down by a [House Redoran](/wiki/Lore:House_Redoran "Lore:House Redoran") scribe and ended up as the book *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*. Once you have reached level 36, reading the book will start the miscellaneous objective to find Haknir's treasure. There are a total of eleven copies of the book on Solstheim. Please see [this section](#Deathbrand_Locations) for a complete list of locations. It is also possible to initiate the quest by asking about the latest rumors from [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") at the Retching Netch, who will mark the site on your map upon inquiring.

_02.jpg)

*"Boss said to bring you back or bring back your corpse."*

Additionally, you may overhear an [argument](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Arguing_about_Haknir "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness between a female [pirate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate") and a male [pirate mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Mage "Skyrim:Pirate Mage"):

:   **Pirate**: *"I told him 'no' once already."*
:   **Pirate Mage**: *"We've got work to do."*
:   **Pirate**: *"I'm not chasing that map. It's a fool's errand. I'm done. Leave me alone."*
:   **Pirate Mage**: *"Boss said to bring you back or bring back your corpse."*
:   **Pirate**: *"Is that so? Well, you'll never get that treasure now!"*
:   **Pirate Mage**: *"Time to die!"*

After their argument, they will attack each other over the discussed treasure. If you stand aside during their fight, the pirate may lose the battle, and you can loot a copy of the book from her corpse.

### The Silent Scream

According to the book, [Garuk Windrime](/wiki/Skyrim:Garuk_Windrime "Skyrim:Garuk Windrime") and the rest of the crew arrived on a shoal in northern Solstheim, where they started digging the hole for the first of the four iron-bound chests. The same night, Garuk's heart was filled with greed; he opened the chest, took out the helm within and placed it on his head... and then began to scream. Although it remains unclear what happened to Garuk, it is said that his scream can still be heard on that same shoal, on moonlit nights.

_03.jpg)

*"I told you. Just where the map said it would be."*

After reading the book, a map marker will point you towards [Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal"), a small campsite along the coast in northeastern Solstheim. Travel to the camp and you will find it inhabited by [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate") and their [captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Captain "Skyrim:Pirate Captain"). If you manage to sneak up on the camp, you can overhear their conversation:

:   **Pirate**: *"See? I told you. Just where the map said it would be."*
:   **Captain**: *"We don't even know what's inside. And besides, there's... the curse."*
:   **Pirate**: *"Don't tell me you believe that rot! Well, as soon as Jorn gets back, you'll see. You'll see."*

From here, it is possible to kill the pirate captain and his followers or simply pickpocket the captain and steal the [Deathbrand Treasure Map](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Treasure_Map "Skyrim:Deathbrand Treasure Map") he is carrying. Once you have obtained the treasure map, the quest will initiate. Search the camp for the half-buried [ancient chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Ancient_Chest "Skyrim:Containers") and pick the expert-leveled lock. Inside, you will find the [Deathbrand Helm](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Helm "Skyrim:Deathbrand Helm"), the same helm worn by Garuk Windrime, although the rumors of his scream on moonlit nights turn out to be highly exaggerated.

### The Treasure Hunt

With one of the four chests found, three remain. Take a good look at the [treasure map](/wiki/File:SR-icon-misc-Deathbrand_Treasure_Map.png "File:SR-icon-misc-Deathbrand Treasure Map.png"), and it becomes clear that Haknir's crew followed orders and placed them as far apart as possible. Note that you will have no map markers and will receive no quest updates until you have claimed the contents of all four chests.

Quick Access to Treasure Map →

#### Tel Mithryn (Southeast)

Travel to the home of [Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:Telvanni "Lore:Telvanni") wizard [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") and find the river west of the [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"). Where the river flows into the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Lore:Sea_of_Ghosts "Lore:Sea of Ghosts"), a family of [netch](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch") floats around. To the northeast of the netch family are several boulders in a pile, and three [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") will attack as you get close. Search the area for the ancient chest ([screenshot](/wiki/File:SR-place-TelMithryn_AncientChestLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-TelMithryn AncientChestLocation.jpg")) and notice that two [treasure hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Hunter_(dead)#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Treasure Hunter (dead)") beat you to it, but paid with their lives. Pick the expert-leveled lock on the chest and claim the [Deathbrand Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Boots "Skyrim:Deathbrand Boots").

#### Raven Rock (Southwest)

_04.jpg)

*"We... we actually found it!"*

Southwest of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") is the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone"). Head to the stone and proceed in a north-northwestern direction until you reach a small pine forest, with a family of netch floating around above the water nearby. As you get closer, you will see a [reaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") and a [reaver lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver_Lord "Skyrim:Reaver Lord") discussing the chest they just dug up:

:   **Reaver**: *"I can't believe it. We... we actually found it!"*
:   **Reaver Lord**: *"Well, what are you waiting for? Go ahead and open it."*
:   **Reaver**: *"No, no, I couldn't. ...You open it."*
:   **Reaver Lord**: *"Maybe... we should think about this some more."*

When they discover you, they will obviously be hostile. Deal with them both and locate the ancient chest ([screenshot](/wiki/File:SR-place-EarthStone_AncientChestLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-EarthStone AncientChestLocation.jpg")), pick the adept-leveled lock and claim the [Deathbrand Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Armor "Skyrim:Deathbrand Armor").

#### Bristleback Cave (Northwest)

The hidden dock, [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing"), is located at the foot of the icy mountains of northwestern Solstheim. A small ways southwest of the dock is a small camp inhabited by [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") guarding the entrance to [Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave"). Proceed south along the shore and you will find a tidal pool with some [mud crabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mud_Crab "Skyrim:Mud Crab") and the ancient chest ([screenshot](/wiki/File:SR-place-BrokenTuskMine_AncientChestLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-BrokenTuskMine AncientChestLocation.jpg")). Pick the adept-leveled lock on the chest and claim the [Deathbrand Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Deathbrand Gauntlets").

### A Cursed Trove

In whichever Deathbrand Armor chest (above) you open last, you will find the [Gyldenhul Barrow Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow_Key "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow Key"), and the quest will update. The map marker will now point you towards the [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins"), [Gyldenhul Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow").

_05.jpg)

80 piles of gold

_06.jpg)

[The King of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand")

Gyldenhul Barrow is located on [Horker Island](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Island "Skyrim:Horker Island"), east of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). It is guarded by a few patrolling reavers. There is a Quicksilver Ore Vein slightly to the northeast of the entrance. The door has a master-level lock on it, but the key you found will open it. Inside, you will find a dead [Adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer#Adventurer16 "Skyrim:Adventurer") carrying a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Torn_Note_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Torn Note (Dragonborn)") detailing how his search for treasure ended in the small barrow. He had to barricade himself inside, waiting for a group of bandits to disappear from outside the ruin. In the meantime, he noticed a small draft from behind one of the two [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposits, although his [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") was unable to break them down. Approach the western stalhrim deposit and use your [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") to tear it down. Behind it is a narrow tunnel leading further into the ruin. Unlock the door and enter a wide tunnel filled to the brim with [piles of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")—a total of 80 piles, each worth between 80 and 120 gold, along with several pieces of jewelry, chests, and other valuables. However, as you start to loot the place, a portcullis will fall behind you, so the only way is onward.

When you have claimed the huge treasure from the room, proceed to the southern door and unlock it with the key. Head down the tunnel until you reach a large chamber with the skeletal remains of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand"). Next to the skeleton lies the legendary scimitar [Bloodscythe](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodscythe "Skyrim:Bloodscythe"). Once you claim it, Haknir Death-Brand's ghost will appear and attack you, then teleport away after he loses about 20% health. Members of [his crew](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Crew "Skyrim:Haknir's Crew") appear to fight you, including [Garuk Windrime](/wiki/Skyrim:Garuk_Windrime "Skyrim:Garuk Windrime") and [Thalin Ebonhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalin_Ebonhand "Skyrim:Thalin Ebonhand"). As you kill some of them off, Haknir Death-Brand will spawn again, and the cycle will repeat until he is dead. Once defeated you'll attain another unique scimitar named [Soulrender](/wiki/Skyrim:Soulrender "Skyrim:Soulrender"). It has an added effect when dual-wielded with Bloodscythe. Also when Haknir falls, the way back out will re-open.

## Deathbrand Locations

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow") | One on a dresser near a double bed |
| Another on a set of shelves near an unusable cooking spit |
| [Deor Woodcutter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter%27s_House "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter's House") | On a set of shelves next to some barrels in the corner |
| [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") | On a cupboard shelf near the boss chest |
| [Greathall](/wiki/Skyrim:Greathall "Skyrim:Greathall") | On a desk in the northwest corner |
| [Morvayn Manor Chambers](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor") | On a set of shelves along the wall |
| [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") | On a bookshelf in a room on the lower floor |
| [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") | One on a set of shelves near a table displaying a large map |
| Another on a separate table nearby |
| [Tel Mithryn Steward's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House") | On a small shelf next to the bed |
| [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple") | Atop a small round table in [Galdrus Hlervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Galdrus_Hlervu "Skyrim:Galdrus Hlervu")'s room |

## Notes

- It is possible to avoid fighting Haknir's crew by killing him in one blow (by sneaking with a dagger, for instance). It is also possible to instantly kill him using the Wabbajack.
- Vice versa, it is also possible to pick the pockets of each of Haknir's crew by sneaking and pickpocketing them, and killing each one individually. This includes Haknir and his two cronies, who will appear again after all of the crew has been dispatched. You will get a lot more plunder this way, as after they are dead, they only drop a few coins and a bit of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm").
- The treasure map is filed under the miscellaneous section of the inventory, not under books.
- You can drop the map after the quest is over, and it ends up being quite large: at least as tall as an [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Altmer "Skyrim:Altmer") male.
- This quest is an excellent source of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), as each ghost drops one sample on death.

## Bugs

- Gyldenhul Barrow's entrance door is locked by a master-leveled lock and technically requires the Gyldenhul Barrow Key to open. However, this can be circumvented by attempting to pick the lock while also having the [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Wax_Key "Skyrim:Wax Key") perk, as it gives you a copy of the required key. Entering through this method and proceeding to fight Haknir will break the quest and might leave it stuck in your quest log, as the correct quest stages are skipped over.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=11965)) The entrace door is now marked as key-requiring, this makes it so that you can't attempt to lockpick it, and thus cannot get a duplicate key.
- Haknir Death-Brand's combat class is set to favor heavy armor when his entire outfit is composed of light armor pieces.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.
- The treasure map may vanish when it is picked up.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2dunHaknirTreasureQST / DLC2dunHaknirTreasureQSTMisc stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2dunHaknirTreasureQST / DLC2dunHaknirTreasureQSTMisc`.

# Skyrim:Debate Hall

## Overview

|  |  |  |

| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |

The Debate Hall

The **Debate Hall** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [their servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant"). It is part of the Dwemer city in the western part of Blackreach.

### Exterior

The interior of the Debate Hall

The earthen bridge leading up to the Dwemer city from the east is unguarded; however, once you approach the walls, both [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [Falmer servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant") actively patrol both the walls and grounds. The walls of the city provide an excellent vantage point to snipe many of the Falmer and their servants. The [Debate Hall](#Debate_Hall) is in the southeastern part of the city, with three entrances from the grounds, and a fourth from the [Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station"). As you pass under the arch at the top of the bridge, there is a wide flight of stairs in front of you; the Debate Hall is to the left. The first of the three ground-level entrances is near the top of the bridge into the city, with a flight of stairs leading up to the entrance on the east side of the building. The second ground-level entrance is on the north side of the building, off a large brightly lit courtyard. The final ground-level entrance is at the southwest corner of the building next to a [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") under a large horizontal metal pipe, which will be protected by a [chaurus cocoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") if Dawnguard is installed.

### Debate Hall

Upon entering from the [Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station"), you emerge at the top of a spiral stone staircase. At the bottom, a raised walkway heads west, guarded by a Falmer magic user patrolling back and forth. To the south is a second walkway, with an open metal gate on the left to an alcove containing a lootable skeleton reaching out towards a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v6 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v6")*. Past the alcove to the south is a long flight of stairs leading down to the ground level.

Heading down the stairs will bring you to a large, brightly lit room with a high ceiling and three Falmer servants sitting on some west-facing stone benches. Ancient Dwarven machinery can be seen and heard whirling away in the northeast, southeast, and southwest corners of the room, all protected by metal gratings. There is a fourth servant wandering across the raised walkway along the west wall. The short flight of descending stairs to the west off the northwestern corner of the walkway leads to a door to the north, which exits into the middle of the large brightly lit exterior courtyard on the north side of the building. The second exterior exit from the zone is on the ground level underneath a covered, darkened area to the east. This exit places you outside near the earthen bridge up to the city from the east. The final exterior exit is up a flight of stairs to the south on the ground level, which puts you near the crimson nirnroot around a corner of the building.

## Maps

- 

  Debate Hall
