Deceiving the Herd

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri").
2. Read [incriminating letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(DG) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (DG)") to determine city of victim.
3. *(Optional)* Make it a public kill while wearing at least one piece of [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") armor.
4. *(Optional)* Choose a high profile victim.
5. Kill a victim in the streets, where you can be seen.
6. Plant the [incriminating letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(DG) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (DG)") on the corpse.
7. Return to Feran Sadri for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When you speak to [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri"), he will complain that the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") have been recruiting and give you an assignment to give them something else to worry about: *"You are to make a public show of murdering someone. Do it in the streets for all to see. The higher the profile the better. Make it seem you are a member of the Dawnguard, thus sowing confusion among the herd. Wear [this armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Armor") and plant [this note](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(DG) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (DG)") on the victim."* He will give you a set of Dawnguard armor so you can impersonate the Dawnguard more easily, as well as the note to plant on the victim's body.

Feran will choose the city for you, but you are given the option of what to wear, how to kill the victim, and which victim to kill. After killing the chosen victim, plant the letter on their corpse and return to Feran.

The following table lists only the victims which count as "high profile" for the quest.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Deceiving_the_Herd#High_Profile_Targets_3)*]

## Notes

- Killing any NPC in the streets will progress the quest, even a guard or random encounter spawn. The quest as a whole will be completed successfully as long as you plant the letter on the body.
  - NPCs killed in an interior cell will not count towards quest progression.
- Wearing any Dawnguard armor satisfies the quest's optional objective requirement for framing the Dawnguard—it is not necessary to use the armor given by Feran.
- Feran refers to high profile victims as *"...an important member of society. Someone attached to the Jarl's court, a merchant, a bard, a priest, someone with stature."* However, some of those mentioned will not count toward the high profile option, so be sure to save beforehand if you want to make sure you get the benefits of this.
  - Reanimating a high-profile target and killing it (again) within the required city will satisfy the high-profile optional objective.
  - Reanimating [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") (using [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall")), taking him to the required city, and killing him will satisfy the high-profile optional objective.
  - Reanimating the corpse named "Peddler" from the unmarked "Peddler's Misfortune" location north of [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge"), taking him to the required city, and killing him will satisfy both the high-profile optional objective without counting as a crime, inciting guards or bystanders to attack nor incurring a bounty. If Markarth is the required city, it is possible to do this using spells with shorter duration than Dead Thrall.
    -  This will not work on the [Nintendo Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") version of the game.[Clarification needed - what part(s) don't work?](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data")
- A murder with witnesses will result in a bounty even if you frame the Dawnguard.
  - Killing [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") in conjunction with solving the [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") murders will fulfill both quests without incurring a bounty if he is first lured outside the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings").
  - A bounty can also be avoided with a stealth kill or by killing in self-defense as self-defense is not a [Crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime").
    - Avoiding the bounty seems to always fail framing the Dawnguard even if the armor is worn and the kill witnessed.

## Bugs

- Some high profile targets will not register as such when killed because they may be in a quest alias that gets swapped out for a replacement NPC before the game has a chance to update the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=14812))
  - The following people are affected by this bug and only count as high-profile targets if the UDGP is installed.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

War-Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfberth_War-Bear "Skyrim:Ulfberth War-Bear") | [Ambarys Rendar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ambarys_Rendar "Skyrim:Ambarys Rendar")[†](#intnote_1) [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn")[†](#intnote_1) [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion")[†](#intnote_1) [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil") [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") [Ulundil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulundil "Skyrim:Ulundil") [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") |

- Even without accepting this quest, the objective "Plant letter on *<Alias=Victim>'s* corpse" may appear in your journal after you kill someone from a city.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use `setstage DLC1RV03 10` to fix this once you have gone through all the vampire quests.
  -  Another fix is to get some fortify pickpocket potions or armor and pickpocket the Incriminating Letter from Feran Sadri and then place it on the victim's body.
- You may be able to pickpocket the Incriminating Letter from Feran before the quest has begun.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- This quest can trigger its kill selection setup before you have been told to actually do anything. This can result in killing an NPC in a city asking to plant the Incriminating Letter you won't have yet, or cause the quest to react to [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") kills inappropriately.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. Keep in mind though that using a Dark Brotherhood target for this quest is perfectly valid. All the fix does is prevent Deceiving the Herd from registering the kill until you're actually told to make one.
- You may not be able to plant the Incriminating Letter on the corpse, instead receiving a message saying "Quest items cannot be removed from your inventory".
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Reloading a save from before entering the city should fix this.
  - Read Incriminating Letter to determine city of victim.
  - Wait for quest messages to appear before planting letter.
  - Submitting to the guards and paying off the bounty (if one was incurred) should also fix this.
- Quest may not update if you use the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade") to kill a target with a high disposition towards you.
- All quest objectives may fail if you kill a reanimated corpse in the required city, drop the letter on the corpse, leave the [worldspace](/wiki/Skyrim:Worldspaces "Skyrim:Worldspaces") where you completed the objective, save the game before the quest completes, then load the saved game. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Deceiving the Herd (DLC1RV03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Feran Sadri wishes to sow confusion and anger amongst the people of <Alias=City>. I am to kill a citizen out in the streets while impersonating a member of the Dawnguard. Then I am to place an incriminating letter on the corpse. The higher the profile of my victim the better. *Objective 111:* (Optional) Choose a high profile victim  *Objective 110:* (Optional) Make it a public kill while wearing Dawnguard armor  *Objective 100:* Kill someone out in the streets of <Alias=City> |
| 200 |  | *Objective 200:* Plant letter on <Alias=Victim>'s corpse |
|  |  | *(After planting the letter on the victim)* *Objective 220:* Return to Feran Sadri |
| 255 | ☑ |  |
| 300 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1, 100, 101, 110, 111, 220.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RV03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV03`.

Deeja

**Deeja** is an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatAssassin "Skyrim:CombatAssassin"). Prior to the related quest, she can be found at the docks of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") and [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") are her brothers.

Until the related quest has been started, Deeja will wander around the dock area all day, and may be found aboard the *[Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave")* at night.

Deeja wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") and a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). She wields a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality) in combat, and carries [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), as well as a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic").

## Related Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.

## Dialogue

She is extremely rude to you and will completely dismiss your attempts at conversation.

:   *"You, talk to egg-brothers. Deeja has no words for you."*
:   *"You have no knowledge of who you speak to. Go away."*
:   *"You want knives? You want them in your belly? No? Then you stop talking to Deeja."*

### Conversations

[Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta") can approach Deeja for work:

| Speaker | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **Greta** | *"Got any work?"* |
| *"I ain't begging. I just need a job. Anything."* |
| **Deeja** | *"Shoo! Go away! You get nothing from me."* |
| *"You bother me again, maybe you will not walk away. Understand?"* |

Deeja may be found discussing business at the docks:

:   **Jaree-Ra:** *"My contact, she says [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell") steel is much desired by certain parties."*
:   **Gulum-Ei:** *"I know of a ship coming in from Hammerfell. Some cargo might get "lost"..."*
:   **Deeja:** *"Why should we settle for half a fin when we could just take the whole whale?"*
:   **Jaree-Ra:** *"Patience, sister. Patience."*

### Lights Out!

During [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"), you will encounter Deeja at the *[Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner")*. You will need to kill her shortly after talking with her.

Before becoming hostile, she will initiate conversation.

:   *"My brother told me you were coming. I'm supposed to give you what you've earned."*
:   **So we're splitting the loot, then?**
:   *"Ha! I'm afraid the loot's already been moved. You've been useful to the Blackbloods, though. You've earned a quick death."*

She will then attack you.

## Notes

- Lights Out! originally had a scenario where you could help [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka") and [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") get rid of the Blackblood Marauders. In this scenario, Aldis would help you defeat the marauders at the wreck of the Icerunner. The dialogue branch `MS07DeejaBleedout` and related dialogue for Aldis show that Deeja could be killed, but also spared. If she was spared, Aldis would make sure she got locked up. It's unknown what would've transpired afterwards.
- The cell "RiftenPlankside01" (where [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms") usually wanders outside the Riften Fishery), contains a multitude of markers that all refer to Deeja: `MS04DeejaDocksWalk2`, `MS04DeejaDocksWander4`, and `DeejaDocksWalk`. These markers imply that either Deeja was at one point involved in the quest [Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths"), possibly instead of Fathoms, or that Fathoms originally carried Deeja's name. Besides these markers there's no evidence that shows that Deeja was in any way related to the quest.

## Bugs

- Deeja cannot use the beds on the Red Wave because she is not part of the faction.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

Deekus

Deekus guarding his loot

**Deekus** is an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatAssassin "Skyrim:CombatAssassin") who resides at a campsite on the beach near [Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly"). He is a target for [assassination](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Deekus "Skyrim:Kill Deekus") in a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") contract.

Deekus spends most of his time wandering around the campsite, guarding the items he has collected from the nearby shipwreck. He wakes up at 8am and immediately begins to wander around his campsite. He can usually be found having a quick meal or drink while seated on the nearby chair. After a day of patrolling around the campsite, he heads to his bedroll at midnight where he will sleep for the next eight hours.

Deekus wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). The campsite has a locked chest and several containers. On the tables and near the bed are various [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") and gold, as well as a [statue of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella"), all of which will be counted as stolen regardless of if Deekus is killed. Mind the [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") near the chests. All items found in the camp respawn after a period of time, whether he is alive or not. [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will provide you with some information on Deekus if you ask him to tell you about your contract. Deekus likes to scavenge shipwrecks, and will run away if threatened.

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Deekus "Skyrim:Kill Deekus")**: Slay an Argonian looting a shipwreck.

## Quest-Related Events

Like most assassination targets, you may choose to have a conversation with Deekus. Upon first speaking with him, he'll say:

:   *"Hrm. You go find your own wreck. This one's mine."*

You'll then get three options:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **I'm going to kill you. Slowly. Painfully.** | *"You'll have to catch me first!"* |
| **(Remain silent)** | *"Go away! I don't know who you are, but this is my spot! Whatever's on that ship is mine!"* |
| **I'm sorry, egg brother, but I've been sent to kill you.** (If the player is an [Argonian)](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian")   **I'm sorry, Argonian, but I've been sent to kill you.** (if the player is not Argonian) | *"What? Why? I don't understand... I have done nothing to wrong you. Please, mercy!"* |

If you backed out of the conversation and he hasn't turned hostile yet, attempting to speak to him again will net you a hostile:

:   *"Go away! This is my wreck! Mine!"*

## Notes

- Due to not being part of any crime faction Deekus will not become hostile if he sees you in [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form") or [vampire lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") forms, or if he watches you transform.
- [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will provide you with some information on Deekus if you ask him to tell you about your contract, saying, *"He's an Argonian layabout, likes to scavenge shipwrecks. My guess is he'll run if threatened. Or swim, if given the chance."*

# Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing

## Overview

Deep Folk Crossing

**Deep Folk Crossing** is an ancient [Dwarven](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach").

A Dwemer convector, used for a [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Optional_Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") quest, can be found just across the bridge. With the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on installed, an [Aetherium Shard](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Shard "Skyrim:Aetherium Shard") can also be found at the location.

You can be given the location of this bridge by the children [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(child) "Skyrim:Sond (child)") and [Bottar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bottar "Skyrim:Bottar") in a [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dwemer_Junk_Peddlers "Skyrim:World Interactions").

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").

## Deep Folk Crossing

Across the bridge on the northward path, you will see a stone plinth. On this stone plinth is an [Aetherium Shard](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Shard "Skyrim:Aetherium Shard")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and a Dwemer Convector along with a leveled helmet and sword, which are always a [Dwarven Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Helmet "Skyrim:Dwarven Helmet") and [Dwarven Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sword "Skyrim:Dwarven Sword"), respectively, from level 12.

Approaching the bridge from the south, halfway across on the right is a platform with stone steps up facing due east. Looking from here at the southern bank, you will see a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") directly in front of you. Following the river downstream, you will find an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), approximately level where the path turns towards the east and [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt"); a few meters farther downstream is a second nirnroot. There is nothing of interest upstream except the spring which is the source of the river.

## Notes

- [Katria's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Katria%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Katria's Journal")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") reveals that a Dwemer city originally called Bthar-zel (meaning "allied city") is located at this site. Katria is correct, with the actual ruins of Bthar-zel being directly beneath it and an entrance to it at the end of the bridge. However, by the time of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), the city is inaccessible.
- A short distance downstream, between the first and second waterfall below the bridge on the southern bank, lies a dead Adventurer wearing the rare [Hooded Blue Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Blue_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Blue Robes") and carrying a copy of [The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars").

# Skyrim:Deep-In-His-Cups

## Overview

| Deep-In-His-Cups | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000BBDA0 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50+(PC-0.9)×7.5 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50+(PC-0.9)×3 | | |

Deep-In-His-Cups

**Deep-In-His-Cups** is an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who is [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#The_drunken_dare "Skyrim:World Interactions") and talks to you after you have completed the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember").

He wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") with a matching [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"), pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), and [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"). He has two weapons in his possession: one a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") which can be up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") in quality, the other an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

## Dialogue

Deep-In-His-Cups will approach you in a familiar, friendly manner:

:   *"Hey! There you are, you drunken bastard. I did it, so pay up."*

Attempting to just walk away from him will have him call to you to come back:

:   *"Hey, where do you think you're going? Come back here."*

If you tried to walk away, his second greeting will be a bit less friendly:

:   *"Whoa, not so fast there, friend. You owe me money."*
:   **Who are you?**
:   *"We caroused together with [Sam Guevenne](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), remember? We broke into the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella")? How much did you end up drinking? You and Sam dared me to go into that bandit camp. Well I did and brought back his stupid hat like you said, so give me the 10,000 gold you promised."*

At this point, you will be given multiple options towards how to resolve this predicament. You can attempt to persuade him that he's being unreasonable, and if this is successful, you will get him to lower the debt at 750 gold. You can attempt to intimidate him into ignoring your debt, which will make him give up on collecting the debt if you succeed. You can also just pay up, or decline and make him hostile towards you. If you pay him (either 10,000 or 750 septims), Deep-In-His-Cups gives you the 1 septim hat, then leaves for [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh"), or to buy something for his headache.

| Choice | Response |
| --- | --- |
| **I'm not giving you anything.**  (*Intimidate*) | **Succeed**: *All right... All right... Fine. I thought we were friends, but you're a real jerk, you know that?* |
| **Fail**: *Are you kidding me? I fought off all those bandits. I'm not afraid of you.* |
| **I don't remember any of that. Be reasonable.**  (*Persuade*) | **Succeed**: *Well... all right. Just because we are friends. Give me, say... 750 gold and we can call it even.* |
| **Fail**: *Nice try, but those bandits almost killed me. Now pay up.* |
| **I don't have 10,000 gold.** | *So you're telling me you and Sam just sent me in there to die, then? I want my money, you bastard.  If there's one thing I hate more than a mean-spirited drunk, it's one who can't settle their debts.* |
| **Here's your gold.** | **10,000 gold** *Thanks. You and Sam drink too hard for me. Think I'll take my gold and go buy a nice bit of swamp in Black Marsh.* |
| **750 Gold** *Thanks. You and Sam drink too hard for me. Think I'll take my gold and go buy something for this headache.* |

If you try to walk away after talking him down to 750 gold, he will pursue you and remind you of this:

:   *"We agreed to 750 gold. I want my money."*

Trying to speak to him after you paid him will have him happily say goodbye, once more:

:   *"See you, friend. And take it easy on the wine."*

## Bugs

- No matter how you opt to deal with Deep-In-His-Cups, he will continue to randomly spawn every once in a while, and make the same demands as before. To avoid paying large amounts of money over time, your best choice is to kill him every time you encounter him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- If you leave the dialogue or attack him and then yield, he won't demand the money again, saying that you’re not worth it, making this an alternate way to get out of paying besides killing him.

Deepwood Redoubt

**Deepwood Redoubt** is a large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains only one interior zone, *[Deepwood Redoubt](#Deepwood_Redoubt)*, leading to the large exterior worldspace *[Deepwood Vale](#Deepwood_Vale)*. The vale in turn contains the entrance to [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End"), thus forming a sizable dungeon network.

## Related Quests

- **[Locate the Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old")**: Find the Dark Brotherhood [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Exterior campsite

As you approach from the stairs to the north there is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush on your right. You will find yourself in front of a fortified position, with three Forsworn guarding the top of the staircase: two archers and one melee fighter. Once you've taken care of them, at the top of the staircase are a campfire on your left and a door set into the mountainside that leads into the actual interior of the dungeon. There is a second snowberry bush to the left of the entrance.

Before venturing in, past the entrance and to the west are some stairs where another Forsworn is standing over an altar. The altar holds an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), some [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), a filled random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"). On your way back from the altar you will find a lean-to with a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina").

### Deepwood Redoubt

Icy corridor

Through the iron door you will enter a frozen burial chamber. As you enter, on the right, a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and three [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins are tucked into a bottom burial compartment. Up ahead you will see a closed iron gate. Just before the gate, on the right, is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") rigged with an apprentice level [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from out of the wall below. Opposite this is a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") in a lower alcove with a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") in the alcove above.

The gate opens to more catacombs, with another random helmet on the left before the path turns to the southwest. Just before you reach the stairs, watch out for a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in the middle of the path that activates a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Climb to the top of an icy staircase to reach a large cavern. To the left is a campfire with two Forsworn standing beside it, one of which is an archer and the other a melee fighter. Attacking these two will alert two additional Forsworn archers into the caged walkway above. Once all of these are dealt with, go back to the top of the stairs. To the right of the stairs, climb the rocks on the north wall. At the top is a [dead adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer") with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). An apprentice-locked chest is half-buried in the snow.

Forsworn

Head back toward the campfire, not forgetting to loot the Forsworn killed there. There is only a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") with a small amount of gold and a random dagger in the area under the caged walkway. Beyond the campfire a Forsworn archer is at the end of a corridor of [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades"). The lever to shut off the blades is also at the far end of the corridor. Before this trapped corridor there is an alcove on the left with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack, a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from a rack above and a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), with a burial urn in the top of an unlit brazier also on the left just before the corridor.

Beware the floor!

Once past the archer and the swinging blades, pick up the coin purse, a sample of hagraven feathers, and a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") from the table on the left as you pass. A [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield") is also by the table. Before entering the next room there are three [frost runes](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Rune "Skyrim:Frost Rune") on the floor (see [bugs](#Bugs)); one in front of you, one on the right next to a stone table, and the other next to the wall by the doorway in the southern corner. Among the rubble in front of the entrance there is a partially covered burial urn, on the table are an empty soul gem and another sample of hagraven feathers, and a random potion is on the sideboard next to the table. The doors to the east are locked, but can be opened using the [Deepwood Redoubt key](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt_Key "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt Key") or your [lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill. To locate the key, go through the doorway to the south being careful to avoid the two [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), as any noise from them will alert a sleeping magic-using Forsworn. Just inside the room is a large urn, and a Deepwood Redoubt key and a random magicka potion are on a shelf (unless you have triggered the frost runes, in which case the key and potion will have been blown across the room). An [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") is against the wall to the east. Next to it is a table with a *[Forsworn Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Missive "Skyrim:Forsworn Missive")*, a random war axe, two sprigs of snowberries, and a couple common books on top.

Sleeping beauty

After dealing with the sleeping Forsworn, loot the Deepwood Redoubt key if you did not find it in the first room. In this room where the Forsworn magic-user was sleeping, a couple common books can be found on the bookcase, and a lootable dead draugr is in an alcove behind the shelves. There is also a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") to the left of the shelves.

Open the locked doors in the main room. The doors open into a short damaged corridor with a cave-in at the other end. There is a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") stuck into the rubble up to the hilt. The door onward is to the left; be wary of the pressure plate that activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") on the threshold. Avoid the plate and climb the path, opening the doors to reach the caged walkway previously seen from below. Here you will encounter archers if you didn't kill them previously. At the far end of the walkway the path continues to the northeast to a Forsworn melee fighter sitting at a table in front of you facing away. At the bottom of the stairs, on the right is a medium coin purse, while at the top of the stairs, also on the right, is a set of shelves holding a random potion. To the left is a random pair of boots. The iron door is unlocked and leads to Deepwood Vale. To the left of the door is a burial urn, while to the right are two barrels, one of which contains [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

### Deepwood Vale

Deepwood Vale

Not really a conventional zone, Deepwood Vale is actually a large exterior zone within Deepwood Redoubt, enclosed from the outer world by the fierce mountains of the Reach. You exit into a snowy area with trees all around and a path heading to the southeast before turning to the east. Here the path passes under a rock arch formation, with a snowberry bush on your right. In front of you is your first look at the large fortress ahead. You can see a large arch ahead with stairs leading up to a lookout point; towers are to the north and south, with the structure rising in the distance.

Follow the path as it twists and turns to reach a fast moving river. Follow the river downstream to a dead [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant, and an apprentice-locked chest. Head back upstream to the bridge across the river. Just before you cross the bridge there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to your left. Notice two archer Forsworn patrolling from the two lookout points ahead. Cross the bridge and climb two flights of stairs.

Campfire

At the top of the second flight of stairs is the large Forsworn camp, spread out over three sections. Forsworn are warming themselves by a large campfire just in front of you, and many other Forsworn are busying themselves around the camp. The first tent by the fire has a potion of random healing on the table. A pair of random bracers or gauntlets are on the table outside the tent. To the left are three more tents and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). A Forsworn is sitting at a table and another is wandering the area. Opposite the first tent on a barrel are an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and a random poison; there is nothing of interest in the three tents themselves.

Smithing area

Across from here is a [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") area with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [forge and anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). The tent here has a medium coin purse, a random set of armor, and some weaponry. There is an unlocked chest under the table.

To the south of the smithy are five more tents arranged around a campfire. There are two Forsworn here, one sitting in the tent to the right, and another asleep in the second tent on the left. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") is in the first tent on the left, as well as a set of shelves containing a potion of minor stamina, a random poison, a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sacred Witness](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacred_Witness "Skyrim:Sacred Witness")*. The stairs in the southeast corner of this area lead up to the [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart"). The wooden steps in the west corner lead up to the south tower.

Take the wooden steps to the west first. There is a Forsworn sitting on a bench to your right and the tower is just ahead. There are only an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt") and two samples of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") in this section of the tower, so descend the stairs to the left of the tower to the lower level. In the tower's lower level are a grindstone and a weapons rack containing an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a random warhammer. There are also stairs leading down to your right as you enter. Down these stairs is a table with two healing potions. There is also a master-locked wooden door that opens to the outside.

From this tower, follow the bridge north to the lookouts. First you will come to a Forsworn chopping wood at a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). There is a campfire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), and a rack with two hanging [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") is nearby. The next bridge continues along the wall to a patrolling archer and a Forsworn mage sitting at the table. Notice the stairs heading down into the water. Swim south toward the bridge the camp is on, and take a quick dunk underwater to find an apprentice-locked chest.

Continue across to the north tower. Outside the tower, under the hanging cage are three barrels with an iron battleaxe on top. Inside the tower is a Forsworn melee fighter whose back may be turned to you standing by a long table. There is nothing of interest on the first level, so take the stairs up. Here a long table holds a random mace, a random empty soul gem, and a random potion of healing. You can jump over a large hole in the floor to the north, but there is nothing of interest on the other side of the hole. From here take the wooden ramp to the southeast, back across the river and through the three Forsworn tents. Veer left, under a stone rampart, to a small set of wooden steps leading up to the Forsworn Briarheart.

Boss's tent

There is a second Forsworn here as well, standing in front of three archery targets. The Briarheart is often watching him while seated on a bench. From the wooden steps, you will be approaching the Briarheart from behind. Straight ahead is a tent containing the boss chest. Inside the tent is also a random battleaxe, a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, a leveled healing potion, and another potion. There is a steel shield next to the table. To the right of the tent are stairs leading down to the Forsworn camp. Take the stairs heading up to the northeast to discover [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End").

When approaching the entrance to Hag's End the path turns to the northwest and continues until you reach another lit brazier. There are stairs leading up to the east, and at the top of the stairs, close to the stakes, the door leading to Hag's End. From here you can climb on top of the waterfall, where there is an expert-locked chest with the [Predator's Grace](/wiki/Skyrim:Predator%27s_Grace "Skyrim:Predator's Grace") boots next to it. There is also a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) among some rocks across from the chest. It is possible from this height to Whirlwind Shout across to the altar on top of Hag's End. Head through the unlocked iron door to enter Hag's End.

## Notes

- Deepwood Vale does not exist within the regular worldspace. Although it is possible to fast travel from this location, it is not possible to reach by means other than passing through Deepwood Redoubt or Hag's End. If one uses the console command `TCL`, one can see that this vale is surrounded by an undetailed, unpopulated worldspace.
- Oddly, the Forsworn of Deepwood Vale are likely to flee from combat despite taking little to no damage.

## Bugs

- Only the third of the frost runes, near the room in the southern corner, may respawn. **?**
- You may not be able to interact with the quicksilver ore vein. **?**
  - Entering and exiting Hag's End may solve this issue.
- Level of Detail issues may cause portions of the mountains surrounding the vale to not render any textures if viewed from the lowest points in the vale. As a result, they will appear black.
- It is possible to get stuck in the alcove with the pheasant hanging in it, but a combination of crouching, turning sideways, and jumping makes it possible to free yourself. **?**
- The Forsworn Briarheat may never respawn when the dungeon resets. **?**
- Fast traveling from Deepwood Vale to Solstheim may cause the game to crash. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Deepwood Redoubt
- 

  Deepwood Vale

Deepwood Redoubt

**Deepwood Redoubt** is a large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains only one interior zone, *[Deepwood Redoubt](#Deepwood_Redoubt)*, leading to the large exterior worldspace *[Deepwood Vale](#Deepwood_Vale)*. The vale in turn contains the entrance to [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End"), thus forming a sizable dungeon network.

## Related Quests

- **[Locate the Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old")**: Find the Dark Brotherhood [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Exterior campsite

As you approach from the stairs to the north there is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush on your right. You will find yourself in front of a fortified position, with three Forsworn guarding the top of the staircase: two archers and one melee fighter. Once you've taken care of them, at the top of the staircase are a campfire on your left and a door set into the mountainside that leads into the actual interior of the dungeon. There is a second snowberry bush to the left of the entrance.

Before venturing in, past the entrance and to the west are some stairs where another Forsworn is standing over an altar. The altar holds an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), some [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), a filled random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"). On your way back from the altar you will find a lean-to with a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina").

### Deepwood Redoubt

Icy corridor

Through the iron door you will enter a frozen burial chamber. As you enter, on the right, a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and three [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins are tucked into a bottom burial compartment. Up ahead you will see a closed iron gate. Just before the gate, on the right, is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") rigged with an apprentice level [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from out of the wall below. Opposite this is a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") in a lower alcove with a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") in the alcove above.

The gate opens to more catacombs, with another random helmet on the left before the path turns to the southwest. Just before you reach the stairs, watch out for a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in the middle of the path that activates a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Climb to the top of an icy staircase to reach a large cavern. To the left is a campfire with two Forsworn standing beside it, one of which is an archer and the other a melee fighter. Attacking these two will alert two additional Forsworn archers into the caged walkway above. Once all of these are dealt with, go back to the top of the stairs. To the right of the stairs, climb the rocks on the north wall. At the top is a [dead adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer") with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). An apprentice-locked chest is half-buried in the snow.

Forsworn

Head back toward the campfire, not forgetting to loot the Forsworn killed there. There is only a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") with a small amount of gold and a random dagger in the area under the caged walkway. Beyond the campfire a Forsworn archer is at the end of a corridor of [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades"). The lever to shut off the blades is also at the far end of the corridor. Before this trapped corridor there is an alcove on the left with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack, a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from a rack above and a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), with a burial urn in the top of an unlit brazier also on the left just before the corridor.

Beware the floor!

Once past the archer and the swinging blades, pick up the coin purse, a sample of hagraven feathers, and a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") from the table on the left as you pass. A [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield") is also by the table. Before entering the next room there are three [frost runes](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Rune "Skyrim:Frost Rune") on the floor (see [bugs](#Bugs)); one in front of you, one on the right next to a stone table, and the other next to the wall by the doorway in the southern corner. Among the rubble in front of the entrance there is a partially covered burial urn, on the table are an empty soul gem and another sample of hagraven feathers, and a random potion is on the sideboard next to the table. The doors to the east are locked, but can be opened using the [Deepwood Redoubt key](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt_Key "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt Key") or your [lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill. To locate the key, go through the doorway to the south being careful to avoid the two [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), as any noise from them will alert a sleeping magic-using Forsworn. Just inside the room is a large urn, and a Deepwood Redoubt key and a random magicka potion are on a shelf (unless you have triggered the frost runes, in which case the key and potion will have been blown across the room). An [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") is against the wall to the east. Next to it is a table with a *[Forsworn Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Missive "Skyrim:Forsworn Missive")*, a random war axe, two sprigs of snowberries, and a couple common books on top.

Sleeping beauty

After dealing with the sleeping Forsworn, loot the Deepwood Redoubt key if you did not find it in the first room. In this room where the Forsworn magic-user was sleeping, a couple common books can be found on the bookcase, and a lootable dead draugr is in an alcove behind the shelves. There is also a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") to the left of the shelves.

Open the locked doors in the main room. The doors open into a short damaged corridor with a cave-in at the other end. There is a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") stuck into the rubble up to the hilt. The door onward is to the left; be wary of the pressure plate that activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") on the threshold. Avoid the plate and climb the path, opening the doors to reach the caged walkway previously seen from below. Here you will encounter archers if you didn't kill them previously. At the far end of the walkway the path continues to the northeast to a Forsworn melee fighter sitting at a table in front of you facing away. At the bottom of the stairs, on the right is a medium coin purse, while at the top of the stairs, also on the right, is a set of shelves holding a random potion. To the left is a random pair of boots. The iron door is unlocked and leads to Deepwood Vale. To the left of the door is a burial urn, while to the right are two barrels, one of which contains [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

### Deepwood Vale

Deepwood Vale

Not really a conventional zone, Deepwood Vale is actually a large exterior zone within Deepwood Redoubt, enclosed from the outer world by the fierce mountains of the Reach. You exit into a snowy area with trees all around and a path heading to the southeast before turning to the east. Here the path passes under a rock arch formation, with a snowberry bush on your right. In front of you is your first look at the large fortress ahead. You can see a large arch ahead with stairs leading up to a lookout point; towers are to the north and south, with the structure rising in the distance.

Follow the path as it twists and turns to reach a fast moving river. Follow the river downstream to a dead [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant, and an apprentice-locked chest. Head back upstream to the bridge across the river. Just before you cross the bridge there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to your left. Notice two archer Forsworn patrolling from the two lookout points ahead. Cross the bridge and climb two flights of stairs.

Campfire

At the top of the second flight of stairs is the large Forsworn camp, spread out over three sections. Forsworn are warming themselves by a large campfire just in front of you, and many other Forsworn are busying themselves around the camp. The first tent by the fire has a potion of random healing on the table. A pair of random bracers or gauntlets are on the table outside the tent. To the left are three more tents and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). A Forsworn is sitting at a table and another is wandering the area. Opposite the first tent on a barrel are an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and a random poison; there is nothing of interest in the three tents themselves.

Smithing area

Across from here is a [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") area with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [forge and anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). The tent here has a medium coin purse, a random set of armor, and some weaponry. There is an unlocked chest under the table.

To the south of the smithy are five more tents arranged around a campfire. There are two Forsworn here, one sitting in the tent to the right, and another asleep in the second tent on the left. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") is in the first tent on the left, as well as a set of shelves containing a potion of minor stamina, a random poison, a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sacred Witness](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacred_Witness "Skyrim:Sacred Witness")*. The stairs in the southeast corner of this area lead up to the [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart"). The wooden steps in the west corner lead up to the south tower.

Take the wooden steps to the west first. There is a Forsworn sitting on a bench to your right and the tower is just ahead. There are only an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt") and two samples of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") in this section of the tower, so descend the stairs to the left of the tower to the lower level. In the tower's lower level are a grindstone and a weapons rack containing an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a random warhammer. There are also stairs leading down to your right as you enter. Down these stairs is a table with two healing potions. There is also a master-locked wooden door that opens to the outside.

From this tower, follow the bridge north to the lookouts. First you will come to a Forsworn chopping wood at a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). There is a campfire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), and a rack with two hanging [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") is nearby. The next bridge continues along the wall to a patrolling archer and a Forsworn mage sitting at the table. Notice the stairs heading down into the water. Swim south toward the bridge the camp is on, and take a quick dunk underwater to find an apprentice-locked chest.

Continue across to the north tower. Outside the tower, under the hanging cage are three barrels with an iron battleaxe on top. Inside the tower is a Forsworn melee fighter whose back may be turned to you standing by a long table. There is nothing of interest on the first level, so take the stairs up. Here a long table holds a random mace, a random empty soul gem, and a random potion of healing. You can jump over a large hole in the floor to the north, but there is nothing of interest on the other side of the hole. From here take the wooden ramp to the southeast, back across the river and through the three Forsworn tents. Veer left, under a stone rampart, to a small set of wooden steps leading up to the Forsworn Briarheart.

Boss's tent

There is a second Forsworn here as well, standing in front of three archery targets. The Briarheart is often watching him while seated on a bench. From the wooden steps, you will be approaching the Briarheart from behind. Straight ahead is a tent containing the boss chest. Inside the tent is also a random battleaxe, a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, a leveled healing potion, and another potion. There is a steel shield next to the table. To the right of the tent are stairs leading down to the Forsworn camp. Take the stairs heading up to the northeast to discover [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End").

When approaching the entrance to Hag's End the path turns to the northwest and continues until you reach another lit brazier. There are stairs leading up to the east, and at the top of the stairs, close to the stakes, the door leading to Hag's End. From here you can climb on top of the waterfall, where there is an expert-locked chest with the [Predator's Grace](/wiki/Skyrim:Predator%27s_Grace "Skyrim:Predator's Grace") boots next to it. There is also a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) among some rocks across from the chest. It is possible from this height to Whirlwind Shout across to the altar on top of Hag's End. Head through the unlocked iron door to enter Hag's End.

## Notes

- Deepwood Vale does not exist within the regular worldspace. Although it is possible to fast travel from this location, it is not possible to reach by means other than passing through Deepwood Redoubt or Hag's End. If one uses the console command `TCL`, one can see that this vale is surrounded by an undetailed, unpopulated worldspace.
- Oddly, the Forsworn of Deepwood Vale are likely to flee from combat despite taking little to no damage.

## Bugs

- Only the third of the frost runes, near the room in the southern corner, may respawn. **?**
- You may not be able to interact with the quicksilver ore vein. **?**
  - Entering and exiting Hag's End may solve this issue.
- Level of Detail issues may cause portions of the mountains surrounding the vale to not render any textures if viewed from the lowest points in the vale. As a result, they will appear black.
- It is possible to get stuck in the alcove with the pheasant hanging in it, but a combination of crouching, turning sideways, and jumping makes it possible to free yourself. **?**
- The Forsworn Briarheat may never respawn when the dungeon resets. **?**
- Fast traveling from Deepwood Vale to Solstheim may cause the game to crash. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Deepwood Redoubt
- 

  Deepwood Vale

# Skyrim:Degaine

## Overview

| Degaine (RefID: 0001F325) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | | |
| Location | [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") | | |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(class) "Skyrim:Beggar (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001F325 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013392 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 75 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 60 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleDrunk](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDrunk "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDrunk") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction"); [FavorJobsBeggarsFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorJobsBeggarsFaction "Skyrim:FavorJobsBeggarsFaction"); [FavorJobsDrunksFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorJobsDrunksFaction "Skyrim:FavorJobsDrunksFaction"); [MarkarthDoubterFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthDoubterFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthDoubterFaction"); [MarkarthSilverBloodPatronFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthSilverBloodPatronFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthSilverBloodPatronFaction"); [Thieves Guild No Pickpocketing Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_No_Pickpocketing_Faction "Skyrim:Thieves Guild No Pickpocketing Faction"); [TownMarkarthFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction "Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction") | | |

Degaine

**Degaine** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars") living a cumbersome existence in [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"), the place where [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") hides the poor and sick. He recruits you to steal a valuable [statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella") from Markarth's [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella"), having previously been caught in his attempts to steal the statue himself.

He used to work the smelter for [Mulush gro-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Mulush_gro-Shugurz "Skyrim:Mulush gro-Shugurz") but broke a few bones and became a cripple. His life in Markarth now centers on two things: sleeping and begging—he will even degrade himself to [dance](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have") if you provide him with alcohol. He sleeps in his room in The Warrens from 10pm to 8am and then spends twelve hours begging near the market stalls in front of the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"). At 8pm he enters the inn and spends the day's earnings on mead. At 10pm he staggers back to the Warrens and goes to sleep. The only exception to this routine happens when you first enter Markarth, in which case Degaine will stay inside the inn while [Weylin](/wiki/Skyrim:Weylin "Skyrim:Weylin") attempts to murder [Margret](/wiki/Skyrim:Margret "Skyrim:Margret").

He wears nothing but some [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes"), and he carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and an assortment of [lower-class items and a bit of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Speak to Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Degaine "Skyrim:Speak to Degaine")**: Ask a beggar about money.
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[Quest all Beggars Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have")**: Take pity on a beggar. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have")**: Make a drunk dance for joy. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Speak to Degaine

When talking to Degaine he will explain in his own typical manner that he has his eye on a very special [Statue of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella"):

:   **Did you say something about money?**
:   *"Aye, a whole heap of it. You see that Temple? Way up there? All them women, keeping to themselves. Won't let poor Degaine in, no. But they've got a treasure in there. Gold statue, size of a child. Who knows what they use it for, but I know what I'll use it for."*
:   **You want me to steal it?**
:   *"Well let's not put it like that. Wouldn't want the Thieves Guild catching wind of us, eh? Nah, just creep in and have a go at taking it out. I'll be here, and pay you half of what my man in Riften promised for it. You'll be helping out an old beggar, and the Divines smile on that sort of thing."*

:   **I have a question about the statue.**
:   *"What is there to know? It's in the temple, you bring it out. You bring it to me, I pay you. Now get moving."*

While you do this thing for Degaine, there's a considerable chance you will trigger the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella"), a punishment from the priestesses for catching you stealing. If you, however, manage to steal the statue, Degaine will warn and reward you:

:   *"Give it to me quickly, before they see us together. You've riled up the priestesses, and the guards don't take kindly to that. Here's your share. Nicely done."*

Degaine will then return to his rude behavior towards the customers at the market.

## Dialogue

His attitude towards other citizens is quite hateful and, when you approach him, he will shout:

:   *"Alms. I said "alms" you backbiter. Give a crippled worker a helping hand."*
:   *"How about a septim? Wait, make that two septims, I feel like living it up."*
:   *"Come on, you outsiders always have plenty of gold on you. Spare a piece!"*

When you hand it to him, he will be equally insulting:

:   *"Finally. Now get lost."*
:   *"Bring more gold next time."*
:   *"Tell everyone you see to bring me some septims."*

## Unused Dialogue

Degaine has unused dialogue tied to multiple [quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") he was once meant to partake in. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

### FreeformMarkarthH

In this quest, [Nana Ildene](/wiki/Skyrim:Nana_Ildene "Skyrim:Nana Ildene") would've asked to deliver some medicine to Degaine.

:   **I have some medicine from Ildene.**
:   *"Old Nana finally remembered me, huh? I'll take that. Now beat it, unless you're planning on giving me some Septims. Don't need you gawking at a cripple."*

### MS01B

This quest would've been related to The Forsworn Conspiracy, and centered around getting [Uraccen](/wiki/Skyrim:Uraccen "Skyrim:Uraccen"), the father of [Uaile](/wiki/Skyrim:Uaile "Skyrim:Uaile"), released from Cidhna Mine, in order to get Uaile to stop conspiring with the Forsworn in the city. Uaile would send you to speak with the housecarl, who would let you view records of the accusations made against Uraccen. These would show that Degaine was the witness that pointed to Uraccen. You would then get sent to speak with him, to try and get him to recant his statement.

:   **(Favor) Why did you report Uraccen to the guards?**

    :   *"Not telling ya. What've you ever done for me?"*

:   :   *"Nepos put me up to it. Gave me some briar-thing. Said it would get Uraccen arrested. He's got it bad for Uraccen's daughter, yeah? Guess ole' Nepos got what he wanted."*

He will then continue by saying:

:   *"Nepos made me accuse Uraccen of being a Forsworn. Is that what you wanted to hear?"*

:   :   **I want you to confess this to the Jarl.**
    :   *"Fine. Not like it will matter much. Jarl's not going to arrest Nepos. Just tell me when you want me to go."*

:   :   **(Favor) I need you to tell the Jarl *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*** or **Confess or you won't live to spend another coin!**
    :   *"Fine. I'll confess. Just let me know when you want to head over to the Jarl."*

:   :   **Follow me. We're going to see the Jarl.**
    :   *"Fine. Might as well do this quickly."*

:   :   **Wait here. I'm not ready to talk to the Jarl.**
    :   *"Ah, I'm sure Uraccen can wait a little longer to breathe fresh air again."*

## Conversations

At random times during the day, Degaine can be heard insulting market merchant [Hogni Red-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hogni_Red-Arm "Skyrim:Hogni Red-Arm"):

*"Hogni Red-Arm, more like Hogni Fat-Arm."*

**Degaine**: *"Alms. Give me some meat, you fat Nord!"*
**Hogni**: *"What did you say to me, Reachman?"*
**Degaine**: *"I said give me some meat. I'm hungry, and the Divines know you don't need more food in that huge gut of yours."*
**Hogni**: *"You little twig. I'll snap you in two!"*
**Degaine**: *"Just try it. Maybe a little time inside Cidhna Mine will get rid of all that fat on you."*

**Hogni**: *"Look at you, begging on the streets. Learn a trade."*
**Degaine**: *"Picking on me again, you backbiting Nord? Tired of those prissy nobles turning down your rotten slabs of venison?"*
**Hogni**: *"How dare you. No one turns down cut meat from Hogni Red-Arm!"*
**Degaine**: *"Hogni Red-Arm, more like Hogni Fat-Arm."*

In the evening, Degaine and [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach") will often engage in drunken conversations:

Degaine and [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach")

**Degaine**: *"Give us a coin, Cosnach. You'll just spend it on cheap ale, anyway."*
**Cosnach**: *"Like you won't do different?"*
**Degaine**: *"I'm a cripple. I have a reason to be drinking."*
**Cosnach**: *"And I'm a porter with no shipments coming in. You're not getting any coin from me, Degaine."*

**Cosnach**: *"How did you manage to cripple yourself, Degaine?"*
**Degaine**: *"Mining accident, back when I was in prison for being a pickpocket."*
**Cosnach**: *"You're lying. You're not quick enough to be a pickpocket. What's the real reason?"*
**Degaine**: *"Fell off the top of the cliff after a drunken party with the priestesses of Dibella."*
**Cosnach**: *"I don't buy that story, either."*
**Degaine**: *"Too bad. That one's my favorite."*

## Notes

- When asked for rumors, the innkeeper at the Silver-Blood Inn will gossip: *"Degaine the beggar got himself kicked out the Temple of Dibella. Caused quite the ruckus."*

Delacourt

**Delacourt** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [rogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue "Skyrim:Rogue") and the resident [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). He spends his entire day at [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink"), either entertaining the customers or sitting for a meal. He can [sing](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances") *Ragnar the Red* or *Age of Aggression*.

He wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006ff45 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

He may cheerfully tell you:

:   *"Keep in song in your heart to ward off the gloom."*
:   *"Perhaps one day, I'll write a song about you!"*

If spoken to before triggering [Investigate the Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Investigate_the_Bards_College "Skyrim:Investigate the Bards College"):

:   **What do you do around here?**
:   *"I'm a bard, trained at the Bards College in Solitude. Wanderers like you should think about applying."*

## Bugs

- Delacourt has no sleep package, making it impossible for him to do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
