Dengeir of Stuhn

*"I might be old, but I haven't forgotten that a Jarl's first duty is to look after his people."*

**Dengeir of Stuhn** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"), and [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") under his nephew, [Jarl Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), an Imperial loyalist. He shares his [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Dengeir's House") in the city with his brother [Thadgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thadgeir "Skyrim:Thadgeir"), and his servant and confidant [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla"). Every day, Dengeir awakens at 6am and spends the rest of the morning at home. Around midday he makes his way to [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink") and remains there until midnight, when he will wander home and go straight to sleep. Dengeir wears the [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00086991 "Skyrim:Clothing") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00086993 "Skyrim:Clothing") typical of a noble. He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Dengeir%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Key to Dengeir's Hall") to his house along with a selection of [upper-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Before Siddgeir succeeded him, Dengeir was himself [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). A staunch supporter of the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebellion and rendered suspicious to the point of paranoia since losing the throne to Siddgeir, he perceives [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") plots unfolding everywhere.

Dengeir will be restored as jarl if you help [liberate](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") Falkreath Hold, or if Falkreath Hold is handed over to the Stormcloaks as part of the negotiations during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), while he will exile Siddgeir and Nenya to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). If Dengeir becomes jarl and the Imperial Legion subsequently retakes Falkreath Hold, Siddgeir and Nenya will return to Falkreath and Dengeir and Tekla will be exiled to [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

## Related Quests

- **[Dark Ancestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Ancestor "Skyrim:Dark Ancestor")**: Destroy Dengeir's risen ancestor, the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") [Vighar](/wiki/Skyrim:Vighar "Skyrim:Vighar").
- **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")**: Prove you are worthy of the title [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") by assisting the people of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

His greetings can be:

:   *"I was Jarl once. But I was encouraged to step down when I took sides with the Stormcloaks. It was an Imperial plot, I tell you!"*
:   *"Enemies and ears. Both are everywhere."*
:   *"The war has changed Falkreath, even our neighbors can be our enemies."*
:   *"If you're sympathetic to the Empire, you'd be wise to put Falkreath far behind you."*
:   *"Be mindful. My maid Tekla has been known to pass information to Siddgeir."*
:   *"My nephew has always been handed things, even the title of Jarl."*
:   *"Stendarr protect Falkreath until Skyrim's Sons rise."*

:   **You said you were the Jarl once?**
:   *"Aye, not so long ago. Some'll tell you I stepped down on account of my old age. Truth is, I found out about all the Imperial spies crawling around Falkreath. A few well-placed bribes, and they bought themselves some friends. Suddenly the nobles are calling for a new Jarl, and all the while their pockets are jingling with the sound of Imperial septims. They named me Thane, and they got my nephew Siddgeir in my place. A real friend to Cyrodiil, that one."*

If he is Jarl:

:   **How are you a better Jarl than Siddgeir?**
:   *"For one thing, I won't empty Falkreath's coffers to buy myself fine clothes an' expensive mead. For another, I won't get mixed up with criminals and other sorts who take advantage of the honest folk for profit. I might be old, but I haven't forgotten that a Jarl's first duty is to look after his people."*

:   **Why did you side with the Stormcloaks?**
:   *"You think some Emperor sitting on a gilded throne in Cyrodiil is going to know what's best for Skyrim? The Imperial City's so far from here, it might as well be on one of the moons. And yet the Empire thinks it can tell us what to do an' how to live. I'm no man's fool. I know Ulfric Stormcloak's selfish and power-hungry, but he's the devil I know. Does that put it plain enough for you?"*

His goodbyes can be:

:   *"Mind what you say! The Empire has ears all over this town."*
:   *"Mark my words, I'll be Jarl again someday!"*

### Some Light Theft

:   **You say there's a plot against you?**
:   *"Not against me. Against all of Falkreath. Those Imperial bastards are spying on every one of us. Last night I saw Lod the blacksmith writing a letter. Probably sending word to Solitude and General Tullius. Are you loyal to Skyrim? Break into Lod's house and get that letter."*

:   :   **I'll get it for you.**
    :   *"Good."*

:   :   **Forget it.**
    :   *"Milk drinker."*

Returning with the letter:

:   **Here's Lod's letter.**
:   *"What's this? Some kind of code? "Need as much iron ore as you can dig up...." He's not spying, but it's clear the Empire is making Lod smith up more swords and armor for them. Good work. Take this."*

### Dark Ancestor

:   **What exactly do you need from me?**
:   *"You may have seen the open grave in our graveyard. Most of the townsfolk think it's the work of a corpse thief. The truth is less pleasant. It is...was, the grave of Vighar, my own ancestor, dead for centuries now. He is also a vampire. My family is entrusted with keeping him buried, but recently someone stole the wardstone, and Vighar escaped."*
:   **And you want me to find the wardstone?**
:   *"No. It's too late for the wardstone. Vighar must be destroyed. If this gets out, my family will suffer great shame."*

:   :   **I will see that Vighar is destroyed.**
    :   *"Good. He will have fled to gather others of his kind."*

:   :   **A vampire? I don't think so.**
    :   *"I expected too much. I'll seek someone else to salvage the family honor."*

If the quest is refused and you ask again:

:   **What did you want my help with?**
:   *"Destroy Vighar, my long dead vampire ancestor. Have you changed your mind?"*

Returning after killing Vighar:

:   **Vighar is Dead.**
:   *"My family thanks you. Take this as a token of our gratitude."*

## Rumors

Siddgeir himself will defend his succession, if you observe how young he is for a jarl: *"My uncle Dengeir was Jarl until a short time ago. His old age and failing health caught up with him, and he stepped down. He now serves us honorably as Thane, and to the great benefit of the hold, I now serve as Jarl."* Siddgeir's [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") [Nenya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nenya "Skyrim:Nenya"), who was originally appointed to the position by Dengeir, supports this claim: *"When Dengeir's health began to fail, young Siddgeir was appointed Jarl in his stead."*. The [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), [Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Helvard "Skyrim:Helvard"), also implicitly supports Siddgeir's version of events: *"Dengeir was a good Jarl in his day. Even if his day has passed."* Dengeir's brother [Thadgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thadgeir "Skyrim:Thadgeir") is also critical about the claims made by his brother, stating, *"My brother Dengeir can be... difficult. Take his words with a grain of salt."*

## Notes

- You cannot receive the quests Dark Ancestor or Some Light Theft from him if he has been exiled to Windhelm.

## Bugs

- Dengeir can still utter "I'll be Jarl again someday!" despite being Jarl already if the Stormcloaks capture Falkreath.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Dengeir's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Dengeir's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dengeir%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| FalkreathDengeirsHall | |
| Location | |
| Center of Falkreath, to the southwest of Corpselight Farm. | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |

Dengeir's House

**Dengeir's House** is the home of the former [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") and current [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

Dengeir at home

He lives there with his brother, [Thadgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thadgeir "Skyrim:Thadgeir"), and his maid, [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla"). It is a large L-shaped single-room house. There is only one interior, zone, *[Dengeir's House](#Dengeir.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Dengeir's House |
| --- |
| [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn")\*  [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla")\*  [Thadgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thadgeir "Skyrim:Thadgeir") |

\* These people will be no longer available if the Stormcloaks take [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") and it is later retaken by the Imperial Legion.

## Related Quests

- **[Dark Ancestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Ancestor "Skyrim:Dark Ancestor")**: Destroy [Dengeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn")'s risen ancestor, the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") [Vighar](/wiki/Skyrim:Vighar "Skyrim:Vighar").
- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There is a small fenced garden at the front of the house with a tanning rack, wooden bench and several unusable barrels along the wall of the house. At the rear of the property the area has several tree stumps and a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), most of the area at the back is used by the wood mill which is owned and run by [Bolund](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolund "Skyrim:Bolund"). There is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and several tree trunks by the river running behind the house.

### Dengeir's House

Upon entering there are two single owned beds, where [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla") and [Thadgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thadgeir "Skyrim:Thadgeir") sleep, coming out from the southwest wall, with a dresser between them. On the dresser is a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*. Opposite the entrance is a fireplace, to the left is a food barrel with a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top. There are three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the mantel and a kettle containing four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") by the hearth. To the right of the fireplace is a long wooden table and chair with bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), two potatoes, three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on top. Above the table are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and to [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from racks as well as two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), two garlic braids and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling.

Further to the right on the northwest wall is a set of shelves holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and three bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). In front of this is a long fancy table holding a bottle of wine and one of alto wine, three loaves of bread, a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). To the right, long the northeast wall is a chair and wardrobe with a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") on top. At the end of the room, coming out from the southeast wall is a queen sized bed with end tables either side. The left of these holds a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the floor to the left of it. The end table to the right of the bed holds four loose septims. There is an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") under the bed and an unlocked non-respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items at the foot of it.

Along the southwest wall at this end of the house is a food barrel and a round wooden table and two chairs. On the table are two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Around the corner on the southeast wall is a cupboard holding two common books, a copy of *[The Tale of Dro'Zira](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Tale_of_Dro%27Zira "Skyrim:The Tale of Dro'Zira")* and a copy of *[Flight from the Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Flight_from_the_Thalmor "Skyrim:Flight from the Thalmor")*. There are a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") on top of the cupboard and on the floor, to the right is a flower basket are three more pine thrush eggs.

## Notes

- All dressers, cupboards, and end tables in the location are non-respawning.
- Based on many internal names, the name of the relevant key, as well as its name on the local map, it seems that this house was originally known as "Dengeir's **Hall**" instead.
- If [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") will take Falkreath during Civil War or trading hold from Imperial control during Season Unending, all items on this house are free take without penalty.

## Bugs

- [Berit's ashes](/wiki/Skyrim:Berit%27s_Ashes "Skyrim:Berit's Ashes") may show back up in the residence after completing the associated quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1, addresses this issue. They are now set to no longer respawn.

Deor Woodcutter's House

**Deor Woodcutter's House** is the home of [Deor Woodcutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter") and [Yrsa](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsa "Skyrim:Yrsa") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the south side of the village, between [Oslaf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf%27s_House "Skyrim:Oslaf's House") to the northwest and [Baldor Iron-Shaper's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper%27s_House "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper's House") to the east.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Deor Woodcutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter")  [Yrsa](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsa "Skyrim:Yrsa") |

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). Along the east wall is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), a wood pile, and a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). Along the west wall are two more wood piles. The entrance has a novice lock.

### Deor Woodcutter's House

Deor Woodcutter's House interior

The entrance leads into a large main room with an end table on your left with a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. here are many sacksof food throughout. Against the south wall is a wood pile with six pieces of firewood and a woodcutter's axe leaning against the pile. Above is a wall shelf holding a sprig of snowberries. In the southwest corner is a doorway to a double bedroom. In the middle of the room is a small square table and two chairs. On the table is a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Against the west wall is a crate, a barrel with a mead barrel on top and above it all is a wall shelf holding an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt"). To the right of the entrance are three barrels, with a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") on top of one of them. To the left is a set of shelves containing a copy of *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*. Around the corner is a fire pit with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") and a cast iron pot containing a cabbage beside it. Above the cooking pot is a hanging rack containing three whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid. To the west along the north wall the room continues alongside the bedroom with a narrow table against the north wall with a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and a copy of *[The Woodcutter's Wife](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodcutter%27s_Wife "Skyrim:The Woodcutter's Wife")* on top. At the rear against the west wall is a set of shelves holding two bottles of ale, a cast iron pot containing three pieces of [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat"), an open crate containing two loaves of bread, and two [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel").

Entering the bedroom there is a cupboard on your left with a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and copy of *[Final Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:Final_Lesson "Skyrim:Final Lesson")*. Against the west wall is a dresser with a bottle and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a wooden bowl with a piece of clam meat inside. Coming out from the north wall is a double bed with an end table on either side. On the one on the left is a loaf of bread and bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), while on the one on the right is a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge").

# Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter

## Overview

Deor Woodcutter

**Deor Woodcutter** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") living in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). He lives with his wife, [Yrsa](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsa "Skyrim:Yrsa"), in their [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter%27s_House "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter's House").

At first, he will be found mindlessly working on the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone") twenty-four hours a day. After [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal"), he will return to the village. He'll then get up at 8am, to go outside and work around the village for twelve hours. At 8pm, he'll head back to his house and relax for four hours. Then, at midnight, he'll head to his bed and go to sleep.

He wears a [Skaal coat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots") and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Gloves "Skyrim:Skaal Gloves"). He carries an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), his [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Deor's House Key"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
- **[The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men")**: Travel to the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") to learn the rest of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will").

### A New Source of Stalhrim

*"Something isn't right, Fanari."*

If you return to [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") after the quest [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal"), you will overhear a conversation between [Fanari](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice") and Deor:

:   **Fanari**: *"Don't worry yourself over nothing, Deor. Do you want a head full of gray hairs before you've seen forty winters?"*
:   **Deor**: *"Something isn't right, Fanari. I feel it in my bones and I smell it in the air. Baldor wouldn't leave without telling someone."*
:   **Fanari**: *"Deor, you must be calm. I'm sure there's a good reason Baldor left us."*
:   **Deor**: *"It makes my heart heavy that you don't believe me, Fanari. Baldor could be in danger, and you will do nothing. If you won't help me, then I'll ask the All-Maker to send someone else who can."*

When you approach him, he'll say:

:   *"I am in no mood to talk, outsider. One of the Skaal has gone missing."*
:   **Who's missing?**
:   *"It is Baldor Iron-Shaper. As our only smith, Baldor is very important to the village."*
:   **Did anything unusual happen around the time of his disappearance?**
:   *"Hm, I do not remember Baldor acting strangely. Although, now that you ask, I did see something in the woods on the day he disappeared. I saw two elves in the far distance, dragging something behind them. Hunters often visit our lands, so I thought little of it."*
:   **Where were they headed?**
:   *"South and west. If your road takes you that way, perhaps you could search for any sign of Baldor. The Skaal would be grateful."*

You can also ask why someone would kidnap Baldor:

:   **Why would someone want to kidnap Baldor?**
:   *"Well, there is one reason that comes to mind. Baldor is the keeper of an ancient tradition, the forging of Stalhrim. It is an art we Skaal hold sacred. If someone wanted to make such weapons, they would have to get that knowledge from Baldor."*

If you greet him after you complete the quest, he may say:

:   *"It's good to see you again, Skaal-friend. By saving Baldor, you helped to preserve our sacred traditions."*

### The Gardener of Men

During [The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men"), when he sees what [Storn](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") is doing, he'll ask:

:   *"What is that?"*

After Storn's death, he'll only say:

:   *"These are dark times. How will we get through them without Storn to guide us?"*
:   *"Leave us now."*

When he walks up to Storn's dead body, he'll say:

:   *"[Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea")... I'm sorry."*

## Dialogue

When you free him from the Wind Stone, he'll say:

:   *"Thank you, my friend. You have set us free."*

When conversed during his walk back to the village, he'll say:

:   *"A fever must have taken me. What else could explain this?"*
:   *"I don't mean to be rude outsider, but I must get back to the village."*

Back at the village, when approached he can say:

:   *"The ash from the Red Mountain has made the land sick."*
:   *"It is the will of the All-Maker that we cut firewood only from the dead trees."*
:   *"As the beasts of the forest provide food and furs, so the trees of the forest provide fire."*
:   *"All that the Skaal need can be found in the land and the water."*

After [Lost Legacy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legacy "Skyrim:Lost Legacy"), he'll say:

:   *"Whatever you and [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") found in the old tomb, he is very excited about it."*

### Conversations

Deor may have some random conversations with his wife or [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood"):

:   **Deor**: *"There was a great brown bear on the slopes the other day. I could swear by the All-Maker that it was watching the village."*
:   **Wulf**: *"Yes, I know the one you saw. It watches us each night, always moving closer. As the ashfall worsens, the land and water are poisoned. The animals have less to eat and become desperate."*
:   **Deor**: *"We had better do something about it, then."*
:   **Wulf**: *"It makes my heart heavy, to think of killing a beast when we have no need of its hide or its meat. That is not our way. The bear might find food elsewhere. We will leave it alone."*

:   **Deor**: *"I have seen more wolves and bears among the trees since the last dark moon. Something is driving them north into our lands."*
:   **Wulf**: *"The beasts are driven north in search of food. The ashfall in the south kills the plants upon which the small creatures feed. As the small creatures move north, the large ones that prey upon them must follow."*
:   **Deor**: *"If they grow hungry enough, they will turn upon us."*
:   **Wulf**: *"That is the way of things. We must be prepared. At least the hunting will be easier with the beasts so close."*

:   **Deor**: *"I'm in your debt, Wulf. That bow you gave me is twice as strong as the last one I had."*
:   **Wulf**: *"It's not just the bow, Deor. Your arm has grown strong and your eye sharp. You've spent many days practicing your aim. The All-Maker favors those who work hard to hone their skills, as you have done."*
:   **Deor**: *"Then I will keep practicing my aim every day."*

:   **Wulf**: *"Make sure that you save some wood from the pile."*
:   **Deor**: *"What for?"*
:   **Wulf**: *"One of our chairs is about to break. It will need to be mended with a new leg."*
:   **Deor**: *"Very well, I'll take a look at it later."*

:   **Yrsa**: *"Husband, do you know why there's a pouch of spiced tea leaves under the bed?"*
:   **Deor**: *"What?! That was supposed to be a gift! I was hoping to surprise you."*
:   **Yrsa**: *"That is sweet of you, Deor, but you should find a better hiding place next time."*
:   **Deor**: *"If I'd known that I was married to a fox who digs under beds to look for treats, then perhaps I would have."*

# Skyrim:Derelict Pumphouse

## Overview

Derelict Pumphouse

**Derelict Pumphouse** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"). It is located on an island in the waterfall-fed lake in the southeastern part of [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").

Interior of the pumphouse

### Exterior

There are two entrances to the Derelict Pumphouse; the lower entrance is accessed near the water's edge, and the upper entrance is a lift reached from the walkways high above the lake that lead to *[Raldbthar Deep Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar_Deep_Market "Skyrim:Raldbthar Deep Market")*. Three [geode veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Geode_Vein "Skyrim:Geode Vein") are found around the lake the island is in the middle of, with one to the east of the lower entrance, and the other two near the bottom of the stairs leading down to the lake from the War Quarters. There are several [crimson nirnroots](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") around the lake, with one on the west side of the island with the lower entrance, a second behind a waterfall due south of the island, another near the shore by the two geode veins, and another slightly farther up the stairs near a broken pipe spilling water. Farther up the stairs to where they split, follow the path to the right to find two [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") and another crimson nirnroot. There is a sixth crimson nirnroot near the pumphouse that can only be reached from the top of the lift (see [notes](#Notes)).

### Derelict Pumphouse

Entering through the lower entrance, you emerge in a partially flooded room guarded by a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"). Across the bridge ahead is the lift serving as the zone's upper entrance, from which you may access the Blackreach exit from Raldbthar Deep Market. On the right are stairs leading down into the water, with an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on the wall. Under the bridge is a crimson nirnroot and an unlocked chest. To access them, you will need to jump over the pipe to the left and activate the [valve](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Valve "Skyrim:Traps") under the water on that side, lowering the nearby spears under the bridge. A second valve under the bridge lowers the second set of spears, allowing you to use the eastern stairs to leave the water.

## Notes

- There is a crimson nirnroot that can be reached from the top of the lift. It is due west, between two waterfalls on top of a large rock. To reach it, travel up in the lift, turn to the west and walk to the edge, then use a single word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). This should allow you to land right in front of the nirnroot. There is also a patch of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") at the same point. The crimson nirnroot can also be accessed by three words of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") from the west side highrock, which can be climbed from the shrine-like alcove, there's also another crimson nirnroot in the shrine-like alcove.

## Maps

- 

  Derelict Pumphouse

Derkeethus

Derkeethus at Darkwater Pass

**Derkeethus** is an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") and a miner of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Several residents of Darkwater Crossing may tell you he has gone missing before you find him in [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass"), being held captive by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). Rescuing him will increase his [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you.

Derkeethus can become your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") after rescue, as well as a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") and for joining the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades"). He is trained in [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") and tends to dual-wield weapons when not using a bow. However, like [Annekke](/wiki/Skyrim:Annekke_Crag-Jumper "Skyrim:Annekke Crag-Jumper"), he equips a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") as an offhand weapon, and will not properly dual wield like [Jenassa](/wiki/Skyrim:Jenassa "Skyrim:Jenassa").

He wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#0006ff43 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") supplemented by twelve [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"). He also carries some [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Once he is back in Darkwater Crossing, he will assume his normal schedule: he sleeps on a camp bed from midnight to 8am, and starts his day with a two-hour breakfast. He goes to work in the local [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine") until 7pm, when he spends the evening relaxing by the campfire.

## Related Quests

- **[Extracting an Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian")**: Rescue Derkeethus from his [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") captors.
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Dialogue

Only two people back in Darkwater Crossing will tell you that he is missing. [Hrefna](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrefna "Skyrim:Hrefna") will tell you, *"Derkeethus used to take me diving way down deep in the river. I miss him,"* while Derkeethus' friend, [Sondas Drenim](/wiki/Skyrim:Sondas_Drenim "Skyrim:Sondas Drenim"), has this to say about the crossing: *"Those falls... dangerous place. Derkeethus thought he could find some good fish in the pools. Haven't heard from him in a long while."*

If you manage to reach him, he will run up to you, giving you the option to ask who he is.

:   **Who are you?**
:   *"Derkeethus, from Darkwater Crossing. Should have known better than to swim all the way to the falls. Please, get me out of here!"*

He will follow you until you get him out of the cave, when he will exclaim;

:   *"Thanks! I'm out!"*

After which he heads home.

## Notes

- Derkeethus is one of only three Argonians in the game that can be married, the others being [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") and [Shahvee](/wiki/Skyrim:Shahvee "Skyrim:Shahvee").
- He is also the only Argonian follower available in Skyrim.
- His mood is set to "afraid". As a result, his facial expression tends to show this.
- Before Derkeethus gets rescued, Sondas and Hrefna will mention him, but after he returns home, neither person will have anything to say about it. Derkeethus does not have any unique scenes set up with anyone in town, either.

## Bugs

- The quest to rescue Derkeethus would not properly shut down when Derkeethus arrived in Darkwater Crossing because the AI package for his alias was not marked as owned by the quest and thus would never trigger the shutdown command. This would lead to his AI being permanently stuck trying to return home, making it impossible to marry him and stay at [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses"), or recruit him as a [Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") and have him stay at [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"). This would also result in him being permanently essential.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Derkeethus may occasionally follow you to the door of the cave but refuse to exit. Reloading older save points may not fix this issue.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12066))
  - Waiting for the dungeon contents to respawn may fix this.
  -  A workaround for this problem is to go outside the cave, open the console and type `prid 0001B08D` and `moveto player` and then talk to him, this will finish the quest.
  - Another workaround is to try to see if he will follow you through the second door out; both lead to the same entrance, but only one leads out.
- Derkeethus may be found in Darkwater Crossing. He will talk to you as if you're in the cave and thus initiate the quest. He can be stopped from following you by completing the quest through the "setstage" console command.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12477))
- Derkeethus will occasionally be out of his cage, especially if you rest in the area above it. This makes it much easier to take him out of the Falmer infested area.
- If you marry Derkeethus and [adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") a [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), he cannot be asked how the children are doing as he has no recorded dialogue for it.

# Skyrim:Dervenin

## Overview

| Dervenin (RefID: 000198DC) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Dervenin "Lore:Dervenin")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | Wandering the streets near the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") | | |
| Race | [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(class) "Skyrim:Beggar (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000198DC | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001327C |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 91 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 67 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 67 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes | | |
| Voice Type | [MaleCoward](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCoward "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCoward") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHaafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar"); [FavorJobsBeggarsFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorJobsBeggarsFaction "Skyrim:FavorJobsBeggarsFaction"); [TownSolitudeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction "Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction") | | |

Dervenin wandering the streets of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")

**Dervenin** is a half-mad [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars") wandering the streets of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") mumbling to himself. He is distraught over being abandoned by his [master](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath") and wants you to get him to take him back.

He wears a set of common farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothing"), complete with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209aa "Skyrim:Clothing"), and carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") as well as some [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").
- **[Quest all Beggars Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have")**: Take pity on a beggar. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### The Mind of Madness

When asking for rumors, you may discover from the local innkeeper that:

:   *"People say there's a man wandering the streets near the Blue Palace. He seems distressed but he's not making any sense."*

When you first see him it is clear that he is desperate, as he can be found saying:

:   *"Please, take pity on an old madman!"*
:   *"Who among you can help me?"*
:   *"Wait, hear my plea! My master, he is lost between worlds and I cannot bring him back!"*
:   *"Why does everyone ignore me? Why do you turn your heads? Why will no one help me?"*
:   *"The flame of my master burns low. Without him, we are all lost and forever gray... Please, help us!"*

When talked to, Dervenin may also greet you with:

:   *"You! You'll help me! You help people, right? That's what you do?"*
:   **What do you need?**
:   *"My master has abandoned me! Abandoned his people. And nothing I say can change his mind. Now he refuses to even see me. He says I interrupt his vacation! It's been so many years... Won't you please help?"*

:   :   **Why don't you leave your master?**
    :   *"Oh, you just don't understand. Without him, I am not free! Without him, I am doomed! All of his empire shall fall into chaos..."*

:   :   **How can I find your master?**
    :   *"Last I saw him, he was visiting [a friend](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad") in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). But no one as mundane as the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"). No, no... such people are below him. No, he went into the [forbidden wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing") of the palace, to speak with an old friend. Said it had been ages since they had last had tea. Oh and you'll need the hip bone... it's very important. No entering Pelagius' Wing without that."*

Before you go to the palace, you may still ask him about who his master is:

:   **Who is your master?**
:   *"He is a great man, but one rarely praised! He rules twin empires that span the length and breadth of our minds! All know him, but few can name him!"* He will refuse to name his master however and will inform you of this by saying, *"But... he has forbidden me from saying his name. He says it distracts him, and woe to those who draw his ire. But you will know him when you see him. He's the one who made me like this!"*

:   **Why do you need him back?**
:   *"Without his guidance, [our homeland](/wiki/Lore:Shivering_Isles "Lore:Shivering Isles") is falling apart. North wages war against south! The holy flame flickers and dies! We need his return. Oh, but... I'm sure he'll repay you when he comes to his senses! His favor is a powerful, powerful thing. And so very worth any... inconveniences."*

:   **How can I get to your master?**
:   *"He stays in the Pelagius Wing of the Blue Palace. The doors are locked, and only [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") can grant entry. But I hear the maids, [Una](/wiki/Skyrim:Una "Skyrim:Una") and [Erdi](/wiki/Skyrim:Erdi "Skyrim:Erdi"), know how to enter it for cleaning. Surely they can help for such an important matter?"*

When wandering the streets, Dervenin can be found in talking to himself, saying things like:

:   *"Oh, master. It's your time to do with as you please, but what about those who depend on you so much?"*
:   *"Tendrils of thought may wind their way through this realm, but those tendrils bind our reality together."*
:   *"A method to your madness and your madness is the method and the melody..."*
:   *"I found the bone! I've brought it to you but still I am refused..."*

As you find a way out of Pelagius' mind to convince Dervenin's master, Sheogorath, to go home, Dervenin will be summoned opposite him, elated about the return. Sheogorath, however, won't be as happy. The two will talk briefly before Sheogorath sends Dervenin back to the Shivering Isles.

*"Oh, happy times!"*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Dervenin**: | *"Master! You've taken me back! Does this mean we're going home? Oh, happy times! I can't wait to..."* |
| **Sheogorath**: | *"Yes, yes, that's quite enough celebration. Let's send you ahead, shall we?"* |

## Unused Dialogue

Game data indicates another option to ask Dervenin to confirm he needs you to bring his master back, but it is not normally available in game. He will reply to the question with the following lines:

:   **So you need me to bring him back?**
:   *"Yes, but don't try to use force! He's far too mighty. He'd crush you like a clay doll, or drop you from the sky, or simply eat your brain right up! Oh, but he probably won't do those things to you. Probably. Just remind him to come home, and... there'll be no fighting or unpleasantness. Probably. He's just a little confused at the moment, is all. Knowing my master, he may very well reward you for bringing him to his senses!"*

## Notes

- Dervenin [appeared](/wiki/Shivering:Dervenin "Shivering:Dervenin") previously in the [Shivering Isles](/wiki/Shivering:Shivering_Isles "Shivering:Shivering Isles") expansion pack for [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion"), where he was the High Priest of [Mania](/wiki/Lore:Mania "Lore:Mania").
  - For more information on recurring characters, please [see the main article](/wiki/General:Recurring_Characters "General:Recurring Characters").
- Internal game data shows that Dervenin took over the role of a new character, [Gadnor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor "Skyrim:Gadnor"), who was originally supposed to serve as a beggar looking for help in the streets of Solitude. In the final game, Gadnor now appears as a random corpse in [Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave").

Desperate Gambler

The **Desperate Gambler** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who may appear in the [Windhelm Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Barracks "Skyrim:Windhelm Barracks") during the quest [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever"). He will only be enabled if the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") picks him as the contract giver.

He will be chosen randomly from a list of ten people who performed the Black Sacrament and want someone killed. When approached, he will choose between a total of ten possible targets, hand you a leveled amount of gold and blindly expect you to carry out the task.

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0003452e "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0003452f "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries a copy of *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")* and wields an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword").

He shares his dialogue with the nine other potential quest givers; see [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever#Detailed_Walkthrough "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") for details.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

# Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic after killing [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack"), [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") |
| Reward: | 3,000 gold, Word for the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 ([Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro")) |
| ID: | DBDestroy |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** Failing [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | Failing [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") | | |

Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. While in the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") during the quest [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These..."), kill [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") instead of a hostage.
2. Travel to any city and talk to a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards").
3. Speak to [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") southwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
4. Travel to the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") and kill all [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") members inside.
5. Return to Commander Maro and collect your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Complete [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") by killing [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind"). When you are kidnapped by the Brotherhood and brought to the [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack"), kill [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") instead of a hostage and this quest will begin. Astrid has a rather lengthy animation when she jumps off the bookshelf, during which she is vulnerable and cannot retaliate.

After Astrid's death, travel to any city and speak to a guard. Inform them that you killed the Dark Brotherhood's leader, and you will be directed to speak to [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") southwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He can be found in the [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost").

After speaking to Commander Maro, you will be given the passphrase ("Silence, my brother") to their hideout and directed to kill everyone inside. He says that you should "have the honor" of clearing out the place, meaning you'll be going in alone. Even your [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") do not enter the sanctuary with you. However, spectral entities such as [Arniel's spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arniel%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Summon Arniel's Shade") and the [ghostly Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Conjure Dragon Priest") (summoned by the [Konahrik mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Konahrik "Skyrim:Konahrik")) will enter with you, and they'll assist you in the assault. The task should be relatively simple, as this quest will have them spread out between each room (as opposed to them being gathered and chatting when you first enter as an actual member). [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette"), [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero"), and the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") won't be in the sanctuary during the attack. You don't need to kill the [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") [Lis](/wiki/Skyrim:Lis "Skyrim:Lis"), but it will become hostile if it sees you.

Loot what you please. You have access to an [Iron Battleaxe of Chills](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe_of_Chills "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe of Chills") on [Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn"), one of the twenty-four "unusual gems" or Stones of Barenziah needed for the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned"), the Alteration skill book [Sithis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sithis "Skyrim:Sithis"), many poisons lying around, four different soul gems, part of the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout, and the Dark Brotherhood armor.

### Rewards and consequences

Return to Commander Maro in Dragon Bridge, and he will be overjoyed and reward you with 3,000 gold, regardless of your level. He will also make sure that the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") himself hears of your accomplishments. The quest also yields a good amount of valuable loot that you'd normally only be able to obtain by joining the Dark Brotherhood. All parts of the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary near Falkreath will remain accessible and undamaged, as opposed to finishing the Dark Brotherhood questline, where a good chunk of it is destroyed.

Destroying the Dark Brotherhood makes a number of rewards unavailable, namely [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere"), a minimum of 20,000 gold, the [Summon Spectral Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Summon Spectral Assassin") power, access to the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary"), the ability to marry [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri"), the [never-dying](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") [Dark Brotherhood Initiate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Initiate "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Initiate") followers, the Master trainers for [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") (Babette) and [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") (Nazir), [Ancient Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Shrouded Armor"), [Windshear](/wiki/Skyrim:Windshear "Skyrim:Windshear"), and [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero")'s outfit ([clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Cicero's Clothes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Cicero's Boots"), [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Gloves "Skyrim:Cicero's Gloves"), [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Cicero's Hat")) and offer of being a follower. (See below for workarounds on marrying Muiri and access to Ancient Shrouded Armor.)

## Notes

- If you have the [Misdirection](/wiki/Skyrim:Misdirection "Skyrim:Misdirection") perk, you can rob Astrid of her gear before you attack her, making her extremely easy to kill.
- The key required to exit the Abandoned Shack will not appear in Astrid's inventory if you attempt to pick her pocket, but will only appear in her inventory if you kill her.
- If you cast [Calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Calm "Skyrim:Calm") on a member of the Dark Brotherhood, they will offer the same dialogue as if you had joined the Dark Brotherhood, with the exception of Nazir, who will not give contracts at all.
- After you choose to kill Astrid, any or all of the three captives can be untied and released after her death.
- Don't store anything in the Abandoned Shack, as the building resets every 10 days.
- Either joining the Dark Brotherhood or destroying it will prevent further [assassination attempts against you](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin_Sent_to_Kill_the_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions").
- After completing this quest, guards will occasionally comment on your accomplishment. See the [Guard Dialogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dialogue#Dialogue_added_by_Quests "Skyrim:Guard Dialogue") page for specifics.
- Even if you finish this quest, [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") will still view you as his savior for getting rid of [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").
- Even if you finish this quest, you can still marry Muiri if [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela") is killed and you invest with Muiri after she takes over [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure"). However, killing Bothela yourself will lower Muiri's disposition.
- Even if you finish this quest, you can still gain access to the Ancient Shrouded Armor set in [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End") by resurrecting the Assassin with [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") or via the [Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone"), or by clipping through the stone door.
- Ironically, killing Astrid during "With Friends Like These..." causes her to say "Well done..." right before this quest begins.

## Bugs

- The quest may not trigger upon Astrid's death. **?**
  -  Typing `setstage dbdestroy 10` in the console resolves this problem, and starts this quest.
- You still might not be able to gain entrance to the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary after speaking with Commander Maro. **?**
- Completing this quest may prevent the [Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim") quest from progressing beyond the [Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)"), with [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") repeatedly stating that they cannot move on Solitude while [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici")'s [wedding](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") is in progress. **?**
- If you finish this quest, [Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril "Skyrim:Maluril")'s [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Maluril's Journal") may still be present in [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), even though he'll never be there himself.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, addresses this issue. His journal will no longer be present if he isn't there.

## Quest Stages

| Destroy the Dark Brotherhood! (DBDestroy) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I have killed Astrid, the leader of the Dark Brotherhood. I should report her death to a guard. *Objective 10:* Report Astrid's death to a guard |
| 20 |  | I've spoken to a guard about Astrid's death. He told me I should share this information with Commander Maro, in the village of Dragon Bridge. *Objective 20:* Speak with Commander Maro |
| 30 |  | Commander Maro has tasked me with killing every assassin in the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary! He has provided me with the pass phrase that will allow me to enter. *Objective 30:* Kill everyone in the Sanctuary! |
| 40 |  | I have killed every assassin in the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary. I should now report back to Commander Maro. *Objective 40:* Report back to Commander Maro |
| 200 | ☑ | After killing Astrid, the leader of the Dark Brotherhood, I was commissioned by Commander Maro to wipe out the assassins' Sanctuary. I did so, and was rewarded for my efforts. Of course, it will now be impossible for me to join the shadowy organization... |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 35, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBDestroy stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBDestroy`.

# Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [PrometheusTheElf](/w/index.php?title=User:PrometheusTheElf&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:PrometheusTheElf (page does not exist)"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [PrometheusTheElf](/w/index.php?title=User:PrometheusTheElf&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:PrometheusTheElf (page does not exist)"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

| Quest Giver: | [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") or [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth") |

| Difficulty: | Hard |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment") (Vampire Side only) |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment") (Vampire Side only) | | |

The Hunters become the Prey

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") or [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth").
2. Kill the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") leaders at [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard").
3. Return to Garan or Fura.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After completing [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment"), [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi") or [Fura Bloodmouth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fura_Bloodmouth "Skyrim:Fura Bloodmouth") in [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") may offer this quest. You will be asked to kill the leaders of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") to "avoid an all-out war". Upon nearing [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") in [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon"), several Dawnguard members will turn hostile and attack you. Make your way into the fort. It is best to try and kill the leaders as stealthily as possible because in groups they can be difficult to defeat. [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") also uses a powerful spell called [Stendarr's Aura](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Aura "Skyrim:Stendarr's Aura") that will drain your health if you come into melee range, but only if you are a vampire. Once you have defeated the leaders of the Dawnguard, return to Garan or Fura for your reward. He or she will congratulate you on killing the leaders of the Dawnguard, but comment that the Dawnguard will still remain active even with its leaders dead.

## Notes

- All NPCs within Fort Dawnguard must be eliminated in order to complete this mission. There are eight in total: [Agmaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Agmaer "Skyrim:Agmaer"), [Beleval](/wiki/Skyrim:Beleval "Skyrim:Beleval"), [Celann](/wiki/Skyrim:Celann "Skyrim:Celann"), [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak"), [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius"), [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar"), [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"), and [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard").
- It is not required that you kill the Dawnguard members patrolling outside the Fort. [Sceolang](/wiki/Skyrim:Sceolang "Skyrim:Sceolang") and [Bran](/wiki/Skyrim:Bran "Skyrim:Bran") also don't need to be killed.
- During this quest, Isran, Sorine Jurard, Florentius Baenius and Gunmar is no longer considered essential and can be killed.
- The Dawnguard members will be unaware of your presence at first, but once they're alerted, they will immediately attack on sight due to you being a Vampire Lord. This is despite the fact that Isran met you during [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)") and sent you to [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt") during [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening"), indicating he must have assumed that you became a vampire yourself, forcing him to rebuild the order alone.
- You can use [Calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Calm "Skyrim:Calm") or [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(spell) "Skyrim:Pacify (spell)") on [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") and [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") to buy the [new Restoration spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Magic#Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Dawnguard Magic") and [bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolt "Skyrim:Bolt") from them. This can be repeated until they are killed.

## Bugs

- Both Garan and Fura refer to Fort Dawnguard being in the Reach, when it's actually in the Rift.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.3, fixes this bug.
- The bodies of the Dawnguard members are never cleaned up once this quest is finished.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- Celann may have 15 crossbows on his corpse, which is clearly an error as it was a copypasta matching the amount of steel bolts he's given.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- Isran's "essential" flag might not get removed, meaning he can't be killed.
  - Use the `setstage DLC1RV10 100` or `setstage DLC1VQ01MiscObjective 250` console command to bypass this.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RV10 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV10`.

# Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Viperesque](/w/index.php?title=User:Viperesque&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:Viperesque (page does not exist)"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | [Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Fire Storm") spell tome, ability to purchase Master level [Destruction spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Spells "Skyrim:Destruction Spells") |
| ID: | MGRitual01 |
| Required Level: | [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") 100 (see [bugs](#Bugs)) |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |

Uncover the secrets of the Power of the Elements

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"), who will give you a [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Power_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Power of the Elements").
2. Visit [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins"), activate the pedestal and cast a [flame spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Fire Damage") on it.
3. Visit [North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch"), same as before, but casting a [frost spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Frost Damage").
4. Visit [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout"), same as before, but casting a [shock spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Shock Damage").
5. Learn the spell contained within the book.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Once your [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill reaches 100 (see [bugs](#Bugs)), a new conversation option opens up with [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"), the Destruction trainer at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") ("What else is there to be learned about Destruction magic?"). Selecting this option will result in Faralda giving you the book [Power of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Power_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Power of the Elements"). The incomplete book contains only a clue in the form of a poem:

:   *Northward, haunted northern coastline*
:   *And south, Dwemer live and toil,*
:   *A simple place, a shield from draft.*
:   *At this stand wield mage's craft*
:   *So fierce the sea will boil.*

This clue points to [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins"), a small barrow just southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). Inside the barrow is a pedestal upon which you can place the book. Once you have done so, cast any [fire spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Fire Damage") at either the book or pedestal. A small explosion will occur. Pick up the book again and you will notice that it has acquired a new page:

:   *Under Greybeards' morning shadow*
:   *At this northern watch, long lost*
:   *Nirn's hoary Throat does scrape the sky.*
:   *Here unleash a chilling cry*
:   *And gild this stand with frost.*

The second pedestal is found at [North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch"), another barrow on the southwestern slope of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), not far northeast of the starting town of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). It is easiest to get there from [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock"), as it is within sight of the fast travel point. The pedestal is on a stone lookout post. This time, cast any [frost spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Frost Damage") at the book or pedestal to receive the next clue:

:   *Over western river waters,*
:   *By Karth bounded, south and north*
:   *On mountains sits a humble crown.*
:   *Sky's wrath on this stand bring forth*
:   *To shake these snowcaps down.*

This final clue points to [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout"), another small barrow near [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") and north of [Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire") in [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") (east and slightly north of Markarth, directly East across the gorge from [The Lover Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover_Stone "Skyrim:The Lover Stone")). The pedestal is on the other side of the stone building. Casting any [lightning spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Shock Damage") at the book or pedestal completes it.

Pick up the book and read it to complete the quest. It will give you the spell "Fire Storm". The final entry after receiving the spell is:

:   *Elemental magic wielded,*
:   *Elemental thoughts displayed.*
:   *Havoc wrought as if for sport,*
:   *Efforts to impress fall short.*
:   *I'll merely use a blade.*

:   *Seeking study, wanting learning,*
:   *Recklessly aroused my rage!*
:   *My pupil you would be, or more?*
:   *Presume not of Shalidor,*
:   *You feeble, foolish mage!*

:   *Quickly dispatched, worthless weakling,*
:   *Though this tome I gladly claim.*
:   *A diamond in the rough, I find,*
:   *Shining gem from feeble mind.*
:   *Now die, and curse my name!*

### Rewards

- Reading the completed book grants you the [Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Spells#Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Destruction Spells") spell.
- Once you have completed this quest, Faralda will sell spell tomes for the other two Master-level Destruction spells ([Lightning Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Spells#Lightning_Storm "Skyrim:Destruction Spells") and [Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Spells#Blizzard "Skyrim:Destruction Spells")).

## Notes

- As [dragon shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") are technically spells, they can be used to activate the pedestals.

## Bugs

- The quest only requires a skill level of 90, but Faralda's opening dialogue has a requirement of level 100, which is inconsistent with the quest and the other master level quests.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- There is a known bug in the lightning spell part of the quest where the book will not appear after casting a lightning spell and activating the pedestal.
  - To fix any bugs, cast the lowest available spell at the book, especially for lightning ([Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks")).
  - The bug may actually be with the frost spell not activating properly, even if it appears to have done (the stage being marked as completed in the journal). If you return to North Skybound Watch and redo the frost spell altar, and then return to Four Skull Lookout, it should work.
- The completed quest journal entry may not appear as the latest finished quest but will be in order the moment you receive the book from Faralda. **?**
-  There is an error in the French translation of the game. After you use the frost spell, the third page leads you to the "eastern river waters" instead of "western river waters". **?**
-  In the Polish translation, the quest objective asks to read the book instead of completing it.

## Quest Stages

| Destruction Ritual Spell (MGRitual01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've asked Faralda about additional training in Destruction. She gave me a book called "Power of the Elements" and hinted that it could lead me to new, powerful spells. I should examine the book to see what I can learn. *Objective 10:* Complete the book Powers of the Elements |
| 200 | ☑ | I have followed the clues in Power of the Elements, allowing me to finish the book. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRitual01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRitual01`.

# Skyrim:Dexion Evicus

## Overview

| Dexion Evicus (RefID: [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")007B88) | | | |
